Continued Discovery of Two Artillery Shells in the Strange Warship Firing Case 95

The shells definitely have the characters "Taisho Year" on them.

The Changshu County Government has already sent the shells to the province.

Changshu News: Suddenly, on the afternoon of the 27th of last month, two gray warships passed by the Gaopu Estuary in the sixth district of this county. Unexpectedly, they opened fire on the shore with machine guns for about half an hour and fired dozens of cannons, causing panic. However, due to the heavy fog in the river, it was impossible to identify which country's warships they were. Subsequently, the police team stationed in the old Wushi Town recovered two artillery shells. The shells only had the marks "Wu", "Ke", and "　", making it difficult to identify them. The county sent police to send the shells to the provincial government for review. After this incident occurred, it attracted attention from all sides, and there were various rumors in the interior. A few days ago, the Zhenyu patrol ship Captain Ji reported that it might have been the Navy Survey Bureau firing on Tan Sha, but the Survey Bureau has now published a denial in the newspaper. Therefore, it is still difficult to guess which warship fired the shells and what their intentions were. On the 30th, the old Wushi District Office in the sixth district, due to the many shells fired by the warship that day, and the inevitable presence of remaining shells in the fields, which would cause future harm, ordered a detailed search. As expected, in the afternoon of that day, one shell was found in Tangyouche, and at the same time, Chen Zhengyang, a resident of the Nianbu Bridge, also found one shell. They were immediately sent to the district office, and Xu Shimin, an official from the district, was dispatched to send them to the county government. Upon inspection, one shell had already exploded (see the diagram of the shell on the right). The bottom was detached, the shell was one foot and one inch long, with 16 bee-like holes on the top and yellow soft paper attached to the bottom in a long oval shape, with printed numbers on it, but most of it was blurry. Upon inspection, the lower corners on both sides had "... Factory Weighing", with "Explosive Filling", "Shell Body", "A", and "75厶" printed in the middle. On the left side, there were characters such as "Fuse Amount 754 Tail Containing 厶". Another shell had not yet exploded. The soft paper attached to the shell had the characters "Taisho... Year" printed on it, which were clearly identifiable. Other characters were mostly blurry and difficult to identify (see the diagram of the shell on the left). The two shells weighed about ten pounds. Based on the characters on the shells, it would not be difficult to track down which warship fired them. The county government, because the two shells previously obtained did not have clear markings and could not prove which country's warship they were, now believes that the two shells with clear characters are of great importance. Therefore, Chen Fusheng, a bailiff, was sent again on the first shift of the boat on the 2nd to send the shells to the provincial government for future negotiations. At 10 PM on the evening of the 1st, the reporter went to the county government to visit County Magistrate Zhou Heng, but Zhou had returned to his residence. The Secretary-General was seen instead, and what he said was the same as above. He also said that the documents submitted to the province had already been drafted, which roughly stated, "The previously obtained shells have already been sent to the province. The two shells now obtained have characters such as 'Taisho... Year', which is sufficient to prove that the firing on the 27th was not the Navy Survey Bureau's shooting at Tan Sha, as stated by Captain Ji of the Zhenyu patrol ship."

Explanation of Artillery Shell Markings 96

(1) The arrow on the right shell points to the characters "Shell Body·7A 75厶·Explosive Filling 7A 75厶·Fuse Amount 75 Tail Containing 厶·Factory Weighing".

(2) The arrow on the left shell points to the characters "Taisho Year".

The Third Route Army Recaptures Guangchang County Town Chen Cheng Telegraphed the Course of the Battle More Than 6,000 Bandits Killed or Wounded More Than 1,000 Bandit Officers and Soldiers Captured 97

Nanchang Correspondence, Military News: The pseudo 1359 Corps and the pseudo 5th Corps 13th Division gathered on the border of Nanfeng Guangchang. After our Third Route Army launched a series of fierce attacks, dozens of bandit bunkers were destroyed. In the battles on both sides of the Xu River, bandits were killed everywhere, and the strength of the bandits was completely lost. Our army occupied Guangchang City on the morning of the 28th. Wu Xinghan, the magistrate of Guangchang County, rushed from the province yesterday to take office to handle the reception and appeasement matters. The following is a record of Chen Cheng and Luo Zhuoying's telegram of victory: "Thanks to the time, this route army, with the Luo column along the west bank of the river, the Zhou column along the east bank of the river, and the Fan column as a reserve force, advanced from the area near Changxiang to attack Guangchang City. At 9 am, our various units successively broke through their first line of bunkers and occupied the highlands of Huangnitou, Qingshuitang, Taizi Temple, and Zhonghua Mountain, with captures. The bandits used the pseudo 13th Division to defend the east of the river, the pseudo 14th Division to defend the west of the river, and the second line of solid bunkers, gathering the strength of the 7th Division of the pseudo 139th Corps and hundreds of students from the pseudo Highway Infantry School, suddenly launched a counterattack against our divisions on the west bank, with great momentum. Our army immediately occupied positions and launched a fierce attack on the bandits, killing several pseudo regimental commanders. Bandit officers and soldiers suffered heavy casualties, but the bandits were extremely fierce and stubborn. From Si to Shen, they repeatedly charged us with dense formations, with repeated hand-to-hand combat, the battle was extremely fierce, unprecedented. In the evening, the bandits poured all their strength again and launched a fierce assault on us, making a final struggle. Our army took advantage of the strong wind and rain to launch a fierce attack. The bandits could not hold out, and completely collapsed on the morning of the 20th. The various units took advantage of the victory to pursue. We did occupy Guangchang City at Si that day. A certain division occupied the vicinity of Hedong. Most of the bandits fled towards Xin'an, and some towards Toupo Street. In this battle, more than 1,000 bandit staff officers and regimental commanders were captured alive, more than 6,000 bandits were killed or wounded, and more than 40 light and heavy machine guns and more than 20 rifles were seized. According to the captured bandits, the bandits were extremely embarrassed when they retreated, and their pseudo 2nd Division was completely wiped out. This is specially reported. Chen Cheng Luo Zhuoying Jian Shen Feng Zhan Yin,

Also, it is reported that our army captured Liu Zixiang, the instructor of the 13th Division of the pseudo 5th Corps, at Yunjizhai, who confessed that the commander of the 28th Regiment of the division was killed by our army in Xinqiao. The pseudo regiment instructor Tang Yin was acting as the commander, Battalion Commander Huang Yanbin, Company Commander Shang Tichai, were also captured. The bandit army lacked food and salt, and the hearts of the people were shaken, and they wanted to surrender, but they had no chance. According to the captured bandits, Zhang Shunqing, the commander of the pseudo 14th Division, was indeed shot in the waist twice and killed by the National Army while directing operations on the northwest highlands of Changsheng Bridge. It was also reported that a bandit officer who was bombed to death by our aircraft was seen on the southeast highlands of Zhukeng, carrying a map and binoculars with him. It was said to be a senior member of the pseudo 2nd Division. It was found that in this National Army's capture of Yunjizhai, Guanfuling, etc., more than 1,000 bandits were killed, and 129 rifles and muskets, 6 from Zilai, 1 from Bailanglin, and 11,500 rounds of ammunition were seized, and 3 company commanders, 1 political instructor, 5 platoon leaders, and 114 bandit soldiers of the pseudo 35th Corps were captured. (April 30)

Songjiang Wrongfully Accuses Good People of Theft and Uses Private Torture A Resident of Hougang Township, Shen Musheng, Voluntarily Surrendered to the Procuratorate 98

He accused the township chief of taking advantage of his power to oppress good people with false accusations of theft, and he bore visible injuries. It is said that Hougang Twenty-fifth Tuo is under the jurisdiction of Jinshan County, and there is a township chief named Ni Shoulin who usually intimidates the villagers and makes them afraid. This time, several pigs were stolen from his home, and he initially suspected Ni Sanhe of the same clan of stealing them. The township chief took a handgun and lime and went to question Ni Sanhe. Under duress, Ni Sanhe implicated Shen Musheng, the owner of a closed butcher shop. Township Chief Ni immediately went to arrest Shen Musheng and handed him over to the Hougang Police Station for detention. Shen categorically denied the charge. Ni, realizing his mistake, sent someone to release Shen, led him to his home, and privately tortured him by hanging him up and pressing him with large stones on his back, causing his toes to crack and visible injuries on his back. Still without a confession, he handed Shen over to the Songyin Sub-Station for thorough investigation. After questioning Ni Sanhe, Sanhe said that his life was related to the handgun and lime, and that he was forced to implicate Shen at the time. The Songyin Sub-Station then released Shen Musheng. Shen, feeling that he had been wrongly accused of theft and seriously injured, was unwilling and requested a thorough investigation and severe punishment. After the prosecutor Meng reviewed the case, he ordered that the case be transferred to the Jinshan County Government for punishment.

Jiading A Large Number of Japanese Troops Arrive in Jiading At 2:30 PM on the Afternoon of the 30th Outside the East Gate Bus Station 99

Suddenly, more than 70 soldiers from the Japanese Shanghai Special Naval Landing Force, divided into Vehicles No. 1 and No. 5, and five officers, including Kashiwagi Setsu Akiyoshi Takeji, etc., in a small truck, came to Jiading from Shanghai. Vehicle No. 1 had the license plates of the Municipal Government 12301 and the Concession 5637. Vehicle No. 5 had the license plates of the Municipal Government 12302 and the Concession 5632. The small truck had the license plates of the Municipal Government 9772 and the Concession 5518. The soldiers were all wearing blue uniforms, and the officers were all wearing plain clothes. After arriving at the station, the patrol police reported to the county Public Security Bureau by telephone, which then reported to the county government. County Magistrate Xu Cixuan immediately ordered Public Security Bureau Supervisor Bao Jing to lead the police to inquire about their intentions and ask for official documents. Kashiwagi Setsu replied that he had no official documents and was here for sightseeing and wanted to enter the city. Bao, on the grounds that foreigners were not allowed to enter the interior without permits, and that a large number of foreign soldiers entering the city could easily cause public panic and suspicion, politely refused. The soldiers played at the station for a while, and then took the original vehicles back to Shanghai at about 3:00 PM. The five officers, including Kashiwagi Setsu, insisted on entering the city. Bao then accompanied them while secretly monitoring them. In front of Tayuan, they wanted to go to the Jinsha Pagoda to climb up and look around, but Bao politely refused on the grounds that the pagoda gate was closed and visitors were not allowed to enter. Then they went to Kuishan Park and toured the Confucius Temple and the Tanying Pavilion. At 4:20 PM, they left the park and, returning through Dongda Street, Kashiwagi picked up a brick and wrote the ten characters "Jiading is good, clean, and interesting" on the ground on the ground of Zhu Meiyuan. At 5:00 PM, they took the original truck back to Shanghai. When saying goodbye to Bao at the station, they gave Bao a bottle each of malt liquor and fruit dew, which Bao firmly declined but was unable to refuse, and then took it to the bureau to report the case. Public Security Bureau Chief Xue Bingyang immediately reported the incident of the Japanese troops' arrival in Jiading to the county government. County Magistrate Xu believed that a large number of foreign troops had deeply penetrated the interior, and even though they claimed to be sightseeing, they might be violating the agreement and might have other purposes. That night, he telegraphed the situation to the Department of Civil Affairs.

Robbery and Injury in Panjiaqiao 100

The home of Li Keren, a resident of Panjiaqiao Township in the Third District, was suddenly broken into by eight bandits armed with guns on the night of the 21st of last month, who robbed and plundered at will. Li Keren, the victim, was seriously injured by the beating. More than one hundred yuan in cash and clothing and other items were robbed. He has reported the case to the county government for investigation and handling.

Changshu: Disputes Arise from the Investigation of Provincial Telephones 101

The Changshu telephone communication system has historically had three branches: ordinary urban area shops and residential telephones, which were installed by a commercially-run joint-stock company around the seventh or eighth year of the Republic. This company was registered and directly subordinate to the Ministry of Transportation. Subsequently, due to frequent reports of banditry and police matters in various townships, the local authorities, for the sake of prompt communication, specifically erected poles and strung up urban and rural telephones. They established exchanges in the urban area and larger towns in the east and west, dedicated to switchboard operations. These exchanges were managed by the county government's construction section. The Construction Department, aiming to connect various provinces and counties for communication purposes, also established a provincial long-distance telephone bureau the year before last. All counties along the Beijing-Shanghai railway line were to have exchanges set up, with Changshu included in this initiative. However, since the establishment of the provincial telephone bureau, users have preferred dealing with the provincial bureau because of its faster connection times, clearer sound quality, and lower fees. This has greatly impacted the long-distance telephone business of the commercially-run company. Nevertheless, the provincial bureau's telephone system only has one exchange, unlike the commercially-run company, which can directly communicate with users. Consequently, the commercial bureau and the provincial bureau are as incompatible as fire and water. When the urban and rural telephone bureau was established, due to its county-run status, the commercial bureau had lent the "722," "723," and "442" lines for use by the urban and rural lines. Regardless of location, one only needed to connect to the above three lines to transfer to the township area, unlike the provincial bureau, where one had to go to the bureau to make a call. Now, these urban and rural telephones have been ordered to be incorporated into the provincial bureau, and Dan Bao-ci has been dispatched to Changshu to take over. However, the original county commercial company and the provincial telephone bureau were in the aforementioned incompatible situation. After the township telephones were taken over by the province, a problem arose concerning the previously lent "722," "723," and "442" lines. The board of directors resolved to dismantle the three lines, refusing to allow transfers to urban area users. The new chairman, Dan Bao-ci, recognizing that such a decisive move by the commercial company would inevitably create a disconnect with urban and rural users, repeatedly negotiated. The commercial bureau then sought instructions from the Ministry of Transportation, and has now received a reply, stating roughly: "The county urban and rural telephone system is of a long-distance nature. The company's unauthorized connection violates Article 10 of the connection contract. Considering it is the first offense, no further action will be taken. The three lines connecting to the county exchange must be dismantled, and no further connections with any other telephone lines are permitted."

Changzhou: City Experiences Gang Robbery and Murder Case - Cai Family Near Da Fu Bridge in Wuyi City 102

At six o'clock this morning (the 2nd), the home of Yu Canrong in Cai Family Courtyard near Da Fu Bridge in Wuyi City was suddenly entered by three bandits. One bandit stood guard outside the door, while two bandits went inside and knocked on Yu's bedroom door. Yu, not thinking much of it, got up and opened the door. Unexpectedly, one of the bandits immediately pointed a gun at him. Yu, realizing the situation was dire, threw over a hundred yuan in paper money from his belly pocket to the bandits. The bandits then forced open the iron cabinet, taking nine hundred yuan in paper money and two hundred jiao in change from the cabinet. After hiding the money, they repeatedly shot Yu Canrong with a handgun, inflicting nine bullet wounds, causing him to collapse and die near the chamber pot. Before leaving, the bandits rummaged through the boxes, seizing joint receipts and other documents. The few items left behind were stained with blood. They then escaped through the back door. Afterwards, the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, upon receiving the report, immediately dispatched Inspector Chen Rui and police officers to investigate. They immediately telegraphed all public security agencies to jointly apprehend the bandits and searched the train station and various hotels, but without success. It is reported that the deceased Yu Canrong ran a butcher shop and was a leader in the industry. His unexpected death in the city has shocked everyone.

Discovery of a Live Buried Girl in the Eastern Suburbs 103

The incident of a live buried girl discovered outside the East Gate of Wuyi on the 30th has caused a sensation throughout the city, with everyone considering it a strange occurrence. After investigation, it was found that a boatman named Lu Shi had taken in a seven or eight-month-old girl around February of this year. However, the child recently fell ill, and Lu Shi did not provide medical treatment. On the evening of the 29th of last month, he took a reed mat and hid the child inside, abandoning her near the tomb of Bai Shangshu. Around 10 a.m. on the 30th, Zhou Panbao was passing by the area when he suddenly heard the sound of a child crying from the tomb. He went closer to investigate and saw a long snake surrounding a reed mat with a crying child inside. Several wild dogs were also on the bank of the tomb, seemingly trying to jump in and eat the child inside the mat. Zhou was quite alarmed and reported it to the local police. The police then retrieved the child from the tomb and brought Lu Shi from his boat to the precinct for questioning. The precinct inspector sent the child to the orphanage for care, while Lu Shi was sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Assassination of Datong Steamer Manager in Yangzhou - Yan Zhenfu, Manager of the Datong Steamer Bureau and Chairman of the Shipping Association in Jiuzhou Township, Fourth District, Jiangdu Jurisdiction, Bajangkou 104

Several days ago, Yan Zhenfu returned from Yangzhou, and suddenly disappeared that night. His family was extremely anxious and searched everywhere. On the afternoon of the 30th, a large pool of fresh blood was found on the dike. Following the trail of blood for about half a li, no body or other traces were found. However, his family and relatives believed that Yan had been targeted a few days before his disappearance at Bajangkou, where someone had attempted to assassinate him with a handgun. Fortunately, he had rolled into a ditch by the roadside, escaping unharmed. He had told his relatives and friends to avenge him if anything unfortunate happened. Now that he was missing and there was blood, they were certain that he had been assassinated. They are currently making efforts to investigate the location of the body and the murderer. It is also rumored that Yan had been dismembered into eight pieces and thrown into the river to cover up the traces, but it is unknown if this is true.

Gaoyou: A Bushel of Black Beans Leads to Death 105

Jie Xiaozhangzi, a butcher from Donghui Town, Seventh District, had a gambling addiction. Previously, he had lost two yuan and, unable to repay the debt due to being broke, he stole a bushel of black beans from his home to settle the gambling debt. Unexpectedly, a neighboring woman caught a glimpse of him on the way and made a big threat. Xiaozhangzi panicked and agreed to give the woman a dou of black beans to keep her quiet. However, several days passed without him fulfilling his promise. The woman told his mother, who severely scolded Xiaozhangzi. Angered, Xiaozhangzi hanged himself the morning before last. By the time his family noticed, he had already died. It is indeed a tragedy.

The Provincial Security Department has dispatched the Jiangsu Provincial Maritime Guerrilla Force, together with the Provincial Water Police, to go to sea and suppress them.

Local News

Commemoration of May First Labor Day the Day Before Yesterday - City General Labor Union Convenes a General Assembly - Factories Close with Wages Paid as Usual - Chinese and Foreign Concession Military Police Increase Precautions 109

May 1st is International Labor Day. The City General Labor Union specifically convened a general assembly of representatives from various city labor unions at 10 a.m. on this day in the auditorium of the union's headquarters on Fuyou Road to commemorate the occasion. The City Party Department dispatched Committee Member Lu Jingshi to attend and provide guidance, and he delivered a poignant speech. All factories throughout the city closed for one day, with wages still paid as usual. The military police authorities of both the Chinese and Foreign Concessions took extra precautions. The details of these events are recorded below.

Representatives Present 110

The following labor unions were represented: Sixth District Paper Industry, Sixth District Water and Electricity Industry, Leather Manufacturing Industry, Sixth District Cotton Textile Industry, Sauce Industry, New-Style Laundry and Dyeing Industry, First District Cosmetics Industry, Dried Goods Industry, Tenth District Cotton Spinning Industry, Pharmaceutical Industry, Second District Knitting Industry, Candle Industry, Lithography Industry, Fourth District Water and Electricity Industry, Fourth District Cigarette Industry, Automobile Driver Industry, Pharmacy Industry, Musical Instrument Industry, First District Shipbuilding Industry, Third District Rubber Industry, Postal Service. Representatives included Zhu Xuefan, Zhou Xuexiang, Ye Xianggao, Long Peiyun, Zhao Zhenhui, Lu Muqin, Yu Yaoqiu, Zhong Xiaobao, and others, totaling over two hundred people.

Chairman's Report 111

After ringing the bell to start the meeting and performing the rituals, Chairman Zhu Xuefan first gave a report, stating roughly: "May 1st is International Labor Day. On May 1, 1886, the workers of Chicago, USA, called for improved treatment and convened workers throughout the city, demanding that employers implement the 'three eights' system. However, due to the oppression of capitalists at the time, this was not immediately realized. The following year, American workers held even larger demonstrations and were able to implement it. After the US implemented it, European countries followed suit. Today, almost all countries in the world adhere to the 'three eights' system. In the US, there is even the implementation of six-hour workdays. The lives of our country's workers involve working more than twelve hours, and the wages earned are not enough to support a family. The reason why our country's labor movement has not developed as evenly as those in other countries is that China has been deeply invaded by various imperialists, causing China's industry to decline. Therefore, if we want to commemorate May 1st, our workers must unite, strengthen our own power, stand on the position of national rejuvenation, and break all imperialist acts of aggression. Especially since Shanghai is the economic center of the country, all of us workers should be a model for the whole country, unite our strength, and work hard for national rejuvenation."

Party Department's Address 112

After the chairman's report, Lu Jingshi, a representative of the City Party Department, gave a speech, stating roughly: "Today is May 1st, and all workers throughout the country and even the world are holding grand commemorative assemblies on this day because May 1st is the day when workers transitioned from an inhuman life to a human life. In the past, the lives of workers in various countries were the same as the current lives of workers in China. The American workers first became aware and staged powerful demonstrations, so the 'three eights' system was implemented and gradually promoted throughout the world. Therefore, May 1st has fully developed the world's labor movement on one hand, and on the other hand, it has also promoted China's labor movement. I have some opinions on China's labor movement that I will express here. The Communist Party uses the phrase 'workers have no homeland' to lure workers. However, when we look at the workers in the Soviet Union, in addition to working eight hours, they add two hours to intensify work for the country's national defense and production construction. Other countries such as Germany, France, England, and Japan are even more advanced than this. Therefore, in this tense international situation and with the national crisis so urgent, our workers should work even harder for the country. Finally, I would like to offer two concrete suggestions: (1) I hope that in the shortest possible time, all workers in the city will be able to enjoy eight hours of education opportunities. Although the City Party Department and the General Labor Union have already established more than twenty labor schools, they are not enough to distribute among the city's large number of workers, and the fact that many of the city's workers still lack knowledge should be addressed in the shortest possible time. (2) Since we understand that the reason for the backwardness of all industries in China is the result of imperialist aggression, all of us workers should intensify production and unite our strength to resist foreign aggression for the sake of national rejuvenation. If we do so, domestic goods can compete with foreign goods, and the sales of domestic goods will mean there is hope for industrial development, and the improvement of workers' lives can also be achieved."

Silver Syndicate Undertakes Italian Boxer Indemnity Loan - Ministry of Finance Issued Certificates Yesterday - Certificates Are Equivalent to Ordinary IOUs - Certificate Holders Can Freely Mortgage Them 113

However, considerable restrictions apply when borrowing from the Central Bank.

The sixteen banks in the city, which previously lent 44 million to the Ministry of Finance, originally planned to issue 30 million in securities to recover a portion of the loan. Now, the Ministry of Finance believes that the issuance of these securities would hinder the credit of government bonds. Previously, it sent personnel to Shanghai to discuss changing the issuance to be done by the ministry, and both parties have reached an understanding. The loan syndicate has stopped proceeding. The Italian Boxer Indemnity loan certificates (i.e., IOUs) that should be issued to the syndicate were officially issued yesterday by the Ministry of Finance's Shanghai Office and handed over to the syndicate. A reporter from the Shishi News Agency specifically investigated and recorded the details below.

Issuance of Loan Certificates 114

The total number of these certificates issued by the Ministry of Finance is 44 million, named "Ministry of Finance Italian Boxer Indemnity Loan Certificates," which are ordinary IOUs. The face value of the certificates is divided into two types: 10,000 yuan and 1,000 yuan. When the loan was established, these should have been immediately handed over to the syndicate as collateral for the issuance of 30 million in securities. However, due to the large number and the time required to fill in the month on each paper, the issuance was only completed now. They have now all been handed over to the syndicate for safekeeping. If the various banks need the certificates, they can extract them for use at any time.

Loan Repayment and Interest 115

The Ministry of Finance pre-printed the month and year on the face of the loan certificates, and each paper is different. When repaying the principal and interest, the certificate will be recovered. In the future, the Ministry of Finance will allocate a certain amount to repay the syndicate's loan and recover a certain number of certificates. The Ministry of Finance's repayment schedule can be roughly divided into three phases. The first phase is from January of this year to the end of 1940, with a monthly repayment of 375,000 yuan. The second phase is in 1941, with a monthly repayment of 275,000 yuan. The third phase is from January 1942 to the end of January 1945, with a monthly repayment of 250,000 yuan. When the entire loan is repaid, all certificates will be recovered by the Ministry of Finance.

Utility of Loan Certificates 116

Loan certificates are different in nature from public bonds and cannot be bought and sold on the stock exchange. However, due to the reliability of the funds, the banks can freely mortgage them and borrow cash from the Central Bank to avoid financial delays. However, the Ministry of Finance also has considerable restrictions on borrowing cash from the Central Bank using these certificates. According to what the Shishi News Agency reporter learned from some sources, the Ministry of Finance's reply to the syndicate stated that the certificates could be used to borrow cash from the Central Bank, but the market situation must be taken into consideration. This means that in today's period of loose money supply, there is no need for mutual borrowing between the Central Bank and the various banks. However, if financial conditions become tight and turnover is not smooth, the Central Bank will not be an exception. Whether or not it is permitted is completely uncertain. Therefore, the utility of these certificates is only equivalent to that of ordinary IOUs and does not have any superior status.

Radio and Telegraph Merger - Implemented Yesterday Afternoon 117

Telegraph Bureau Director Wu Baofeng and Chief Engineer Yu Ruxin went to Beijing to request instructions from the Ministry of Transportation regarding the merger. This has now been completed, and they returned to Shanghai one after the other yesterday. Although the Radio and Telegraph merger was scheduled to be implemented on the day before yesterday (the 1st), it was only officially realized yesterday afternoon. The original location of the Radio General Station on Minquan Road will be used by the bureau's engineering department to conduct business. The other three departments, namely the reporting, affairs, and business departments, will conduct business at the Telegraph Bureau on Fuzhou Road. Yesterday afternoon, all personnel in each department worked in the places assigned according to the new organization.

In order to discuss future procedures, Bureau Director Wu Baofeng and Chief Engineer Yu Ruxin specifically convened Reporting Department Chief Hua Shijian, Affairs Department Chief Chen Wende, and others at the bureau at 3 p.m. yesterday to discuss everything and decide on detailed operating rules, which will be reported to the Ministry of Transportation for record.

Selection of Engineering Department Chief 119

After the bureau is formally merged, the internal personnel arrangements have been decided. Before it is completed, the affairs of the Engineering Department will be temporarily handled concurrently by Chief Engineer Yu Ruxin. Li Shijia Arrived in Shanghai from Fujian Yesterday to Discuss - The Japanese Are Plotting a Desperate Secret Attack on South China - Li Will Go to Beijing Tonight to Report Everything to the Navy Headquarters 121

Li Shijia, a member of the Fujian Provincial Government and commander of the Majiang naval base, was previously ordered by the Navy Headquarters to inspect the Marine Corps stationed in Fujian and to suppress pirates in the Fujian waters. Now that the inspection is complete and the coastal bandits have been gradually suppressed, he took the Huaan merchant ship from Fujian to Shanghai the day before yesterday and will transfer to Beijing to report everything to the Navy Headquarters. A reporter from the Riri News Agency visited Li at his residence yesterday morning and asked him about the details of the bandit suppression, the reorganization of the land forces, the Japanese conspiracy to secretly attack South China, and the recent political situation in Fujian Province. He provided a detailed account, which is recorded below.

The Japanese Increasingly Covet South China 122

Li first stated that the recent diplomatic situation is becoming increasingly tense. However, the general public is focusing on Japan's invasion of North China and neglecting Japan's conspiracy in South China. Japan's threat to North China is still obvious, but its secret attack on the South is intensifying step by step, with various cunning tricks, deceiving on the east and attacking on the west. Its intentions are unfathomable and hearing about them is quite frightening. The current situation is fraught with crises, and our country's government and public cannot afford to ignore it.

The Process of Suppressing Coastal Bandits 123

The coastal pirates in Fujian Province were originally very rampant. Furthermore, after the puppet government promoted the division of land, the local communists became even more active. In places such as Lianjiang, Huangqi, Mabi, Luoyuan, Fuying Island, and Changle and Wenao Island, the bandits were rampant. Starting on March 13, when I went to various places to inspect the land forces, I led the various ships to gradually pacify the communists. We successively destroyed more than ten Soviet governments in districts and towns, killed hundreds of local communists, and captured over a thousand firearms. Important bandits have been sent to the province and will be interrogated by the Security Department. There are currently no traces of bandits or communists in the coastal areas.

Actively Reorganizing the Land Forces 124

The Marine Corps was established in 1922. Initially, there was only one brigade with two regiments, which was later expanded to ten regiments. However, during the reorganization and reduction, four regiments were eliminated. There are currently two brigades with four regiments. In the past, due to local political relations, the land forces were mostly stationed in the coastal areas of Fujian Province to capture pirates. They were once transferred to Xiangshan in Nanjing for training, but later, due to the Fujian Incident, they were transferred back to Fujian Province. After I took over the land forces, I decided to thoroughly reorganize them to make them a strong force. I decided to start with education and have established a military academy to train junior officers.

Recent Political Situation in Fujian Province 125

Since the Nineteenth Route Army rebellion, Fujian Province has been plagued by bandits everywhere and the financial situation has been extremely chaotic. Since the establishment of the provincial government, it has first reorganized the militias of various counties, forming sixteen security teams. However, since the reorganization was just beginning, there were inevitably disparities. After resolving the Chen Yucai, Lin Jing, and other units with poor discipline, the other units are currently being trained. Although local finances are subsidized by the central government, the amount is limited and insufficient. The provincial government is now making every effort to economize. Other matters such as disaster relief and local autonomy are also being handled in order. I am scheduled to take the night train to Beijing on the evening of the 3rd.

Peide Lane: Tenant Petition for Water Restoration; Negotiations with the Public Works Department and Water Company Ineffective 128

Since Peide Lane on Xin Zha Road was illegally cut off from water by the owner, Xunshi, colluding with the British Shanghai Water Company, negotiations with the Public Works Department and the water company have been ineffective. Representatives of the lane believe that if this continues, tragedy is inevitable. Yesterday, they petitioned the Party and government organs. Details are as follows:

Yesterday's Petition 129

At 7:00 AM yesterday, all tenants planned to obtain water from the Catholic Church, using firecrackers as a signal. When the priests inside the church heard the sound of firecrackers, they immediately connected the hose to the outside of the door, in view of the previous day's violent failure. Then, they elected six representatives, Wang Jieqing, Leng Bingnan, Liu Xinfu, Huang Yaozu, Zhang Yuwen, and Liu Chengyong, to carry a petition to the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Municipal Party Department, the Municipal Government, and the Social Affairs Bureau to request relief. Zhang Mengling of the Foreign Affairs Office, Huang Yangren of the Municipal Party Department, Xiang Wei of the Municipal Government, and Sun Yongyi of the Social Affairs Bureau received them. After the representatives stated their intentions, they all agreed to vigorously negotiate with the Public Works Department to restore water immediately to maintain people's lives. The representatives were satisfied and returned.

Ineffective Negotiations 130

On the Public Works Department side, Acting Lawyer Wang Xianggu still went to negotiate, but Public Works Department Director Zhong Si's statements all sided with the water company and did not agree to the request, so there was still no result. On the water company side, they were asked to pay attention to the obligations stipulated in the treaty, but they distorted the English clauses to protect the owner in every possible way, so they also did not get the point.

Petition 131

Representatives of the lane presented to the Party and government organs yesterday, stating: "We respectfully submit this petition regarding the cruel and unlawful act of the Shanghai Water Company of the Public Concession, cutting off water and forcing people to their deaths. We request that you promptly and seriously negotiate with the Public Works Department and order the immediate restoration of water to maintain people's lives and protect public safety. We, the undersigned, are the representatives publicly elected by all the tenants of Peide Lane on Xin Zha Road. We have lived in this lane for many years. There are a total of 116 houses in the lane, each with two or three tenants or several families, totaling more than 3,000 people. The water used is supplied by the British Shanghai Water Company, and the water fee is paid by the landlord, the Catholic Church, from the rent. In the 19th year of the Republic, the water rate increased, and each household has been increased by one yuan. However, this is not a fee that the tenants should pay, but they understand the difficulties and have not argued. Unexpectedly, the landlord is gaining an inch and advancing a foot, and ordered the gatekeeper to verbally notify each household to increase the water fee by five yuan. The tenants believe that this is so greedy and insatiable, and it is too unreasonable. They immediately refused sternly. The landlord, the Catholic Church, because its desire was not fulfilled, instigated the water company to send registered mail, urging each household to install water meters separately. The tenants, because they had not received written notice from the landlord in advance, stopped paying for water supply, and the landlord did not fairly deduct the water fee from the rent, so it was inconvenient to install water meters separately. They were also afraid of misunderstandings, and sent representatives to the company to explain and earnestly requested that before this dispute is resolved, if the water fee is refused to be paid by the landlords, the tenants are willing to pay in full and provide reliable security. They pleaded repeatedly, but the company insisted on sophistry and could not reverse its determination to install water meters separately within a time limit. They had to go to the landlord, the Catholic Church, for consultation, but they were also rejected and ignored. All kinds of situations show that they are colluding to oppress and act as accomplices. Although the tenants are weak, if they are not treated fairly, it is difficult to be oppressed and subdued by their improper forces. Unexpectedly, the water company saw that its plan did not succeed, and on the morning of the 24th of last month, at 9:00 AM, it brazenly disregarded everything, suddenly sent several workers, closed the water gate, and cut off the water, intending to put more than 3,000 tenants in the entire lane to death, to show its vicious and cruel means to achieve its private plot of pressing for additional fees. According to a clause in the exclusive contract between the water company and the Public Works Department on March 17, 1928, translated as 'In houses where water fees have not been paid, if there are people living in the house, the water company may not, at the request of the landlord, cut off the water supply to all or part of the house, but the landlord is not thereby relieved of its responsibility to pay all water fees.' According to the original meaning of this contract, there is a restriction on the water company's abuse of power and protection of the public interest. Even if there is a request from the landlord, the water company may not follow the water cut, the regulations are very clear. Moreover, the tenants are willing to pay the water fee, and there is no reason to refuse the water supply. Unexpectedly, the water company disregards the law and does not follow reason, and uses the water on which the lives of more than one million citizens in the concession depend as a tool to oppress and add fees and blackmail at will. If it fails slightly, it threatens to cut off the water. Similar incidents have occurred repeatedly. Although citizens have appealed repeatedly, the Public Works Department has turned a blind eye and turned a deaf ear. In this situation, Chinese people in our concession not only have no explicitly stipulated behavior and are bullied everywhere, but also lose the effect of protection even with an explicitly stipulated exclusive contract. Such behavior not only treats Peide Lane tenants like fish and meat, but also treats the entire concession's compatriots and citizens as if they are no one. If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? If this is not fought for, what can be fought for? Also, because the water has been cut off for seven days, the situation is urgent. The matter of unreasonable oppression in Peide Lane is small, but harming the entire national system is a big matter. Therefore, we present this special report, earnestly requesting your government to examine and verify, and request that you promptly and seriously negotiate with the Public Works Department, and order the water company to immediately restore the water supply, and prevent similar inhuman acts from happening again in the future, so as to maintain the lives of the people and protect sovereignty. This is truly a virtue. We respectfully submit this report to the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Department, and the Social Affairs Bureau with the utmost urgency."

Motono, a counselor at the Japanese embassy in Shanghai, had originally planned to return to his country with Arima, but it did not work out due to circumstances. It is now rescheduled to depart on the 12th of this month. It is observed that Japanese officials stationed in China have been frequently traveling back and forth recently. There must be important tasks in this, and we hope that the people of the country will pay attention.

Railway Bonds Issued Yesterday Morning; Bank of China Purchased the Most 145

The Ministry of Railways' first issue of 12 million yuan of railway bonds was issued yesterday morning at 98% of face value, and was purchased by various banks without circulating in the market. The funds from the bonds will be stored in the banks and paid out as needed when purchasing materials. The bonds have an annual interest rate of 6%, payable on June 30th and December 31st of each year. Starting from June 30th, 24th year of the Republic, the principal will be repaid using a lottery method according to the principal and interest repayment schedule, divided into 16 times over eight years, and will be fully repaid by the end of the 31st year of the Republic. It is said that the Bank of China purchased the largest portion of the bonds.

Maritime Administration: Ship Collision Meeting Held the Day Before Yesterday 150

The Ship Collision Dispute Handling Committee of the Shanghai Maritime Administration of the Ministry of Communications held its eleventh meeting at the bureau at 1:00 PM the day before yesterday (the 1st). Attendees included Peng Hu, Chen Ganqing, Xu Jijie, He Daoyun, Zhang Gui, etc. Chen Baoyan attended as an observer. Peng Hu chaired the meeting and resolved the following cases: (1) Continued discussion of the case of the Hengshan Wheel of the Sanbei Wheel Company sinking the Dingsheng Steamer, resolved: The Hengshan Wheel has not yet arrived in Shanghai, and the wheel's second mate and helmsman were unable to attend the meeting for questioning. This case will be left for discussion at the next meeting, (2) Continued discussion of the collision case between the Chuanshan Wheel of the Chuanshan Wheel Company and the Changyuan Wood Vessel Jin Changsen Sailboat off the coast of Shipu Port in Zhejiang, resolved: According to the reports and testimonies of the two ships, (A) On the Chuanshan Wheel side, after Chuanshan saw the white light and sail shadow in front, it clearly knew that a sailboat was coming. After checking that the wind direction at that time was north-north-west, the bow of the Chuanshan should have been slightly to the left (upwind side) to give way. (According to the Chuanshan chief mate, there were still more than 1,000 feet to the left of Land Mountain,) but at that time, the Chuanshan turned to the right to avoid, and the measures were indeed inappropriate, (B) On the sailboat side, it was said that one light turned into a collision in a flash, which seems to be inconsistent with the facts. The position and direction of the two ships, the sailboat should have seen the red light early after seeing the green light and before the "harmonious" collision, because between when the two ships met (facing each other) and when they collided (almost parallel), the red light should have been seen, but the sailboat failed to pay full attention and take the opportunity to avoid, and only turned to the left, which was also inappropriate. As for its use of gunfire instead of shouts for help, which injured Chuanshan with bullets, although it was not related to driving, this kind of behavior was absurd. According to the above situation, the Chuanshan Wheel should bear 60% of the fault, and the Jin Changsen Sailboat should bear 40% of the fault, (3) The case of the Fuzhou Small Wheel of the Xincheng Wheel Bureau being sunk near the Longjusha Beach Mouth in Jiangyin, resolved: According to four reasons, (lengthy words omitted), the Fuzhou Small Wheel was not sunk by the Jing'an Wheel, (4) Interrogation of Boatman Meng Afu, resolved: (A) Inform the Taikoo Company to send the report of the Wuxue Wheel captain to the bureau, and inform the captain to attend the meeting for questioning at the next meeting, (B) At the same time, send a letter to the Jianghai Customs Commissioner to send the harbor master's report on this case to the bureau, (C) After the reports from the above two parties are received, a public judgment will be made on a scheduled date.

Beijing-Shanghai Railway: Joint Transportation with Jing-Wu Line; Contract Signed by Three Parties; Officially Implemented on the 1st 151

The joint transportation between the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, the Jing-Wu Line under the Highway Administration Office of Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, and the Anhui Province Jing-Wu West Section Long-Distance Bus Company has been approved by the Traffic Department and ratified by the Railway Bureau. A formal contract has been signed by the three parties, and it has been

implemented since May 1st of this year. The stations of Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, and Zhenjiang north of Shanghai on the Beijing-Shanghai line will serve as joint transportation management offices without setting up stations temporarily. The company will use the three stations of Wuhu, Dangtu, and Caishi as joint transportation stations. The three parties will use Nanjing as a connecting station and will only issue express, ordinary, first, second, and third-class joint transportation single or round-trip tickets and luggage transportation services. Packages will not be handled for joint transportation for the time being. For this joint transportation service, children under the age of four will be exempt from ticket prices according to regulations. Children aged four to twelve will be charged half price. Those aged twelve and above will be charged the full price. If half-price hard tickets are issued to children, the sharp corner at the bottom should be cut off for verification by the accounting department. The various tickets, receipts, waybills, etc., have also been produced and distributed by the Beijing-Shanghai Accounting Department, it is said.

Dispute Over Rickshaw Licenses in the French Concession: Progress of Negotiations by the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities 153

Representatives of rickshaw operators in the city, Zhang Huaiyang, and others, submitted a petition to the municipal government requesting assistance in negotiations regarding the sudden restrictions imposed on rickshaw licenses recently issued by the French Concession, which resulted in some operators being unable to obtain licenses and operate. The municipal government ordered the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities to handle the matter. Subsequently, the bureau sent personnel to contact the French Concession authorities. It was reported that the French Concession has never restricted the issuance of rickshaw licenses. New licenses are issued during the first four days of each month (i.e., from the 1st to the 4th) on a first-come, first-served basis. All districts of Shanghai, including French Shanghai, South Shanghai, North Shanghai, and West Shanghai, can preferentially obtain French Concession licenses. The total number of licenses issued each month is less than 17,000. Therefore, on March 6, 1933, the Board of Directors of the French Municipal Council decided to limit the number to 17,000. However, recently, after the war in Zhabei, the city's situation has deteriorated. Many rickshaw pullers from there have come to the Southern City to operate and obtain French licenses nearby. The situation is similar in West Shanghai, resulting in exceeding the quota. As a result of the negotiations, the French Concession authorities agreed to issue an additional 150 licenses, but the Rickshaw Trade Association must first submit the application to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the French Concession, which will forward it to the French Municipal Council. The council will then devise a method to request the French Consul General in Shanghai to increase the number of rickshaw licenses by 150, which will still be sent to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association for transfer to the Rickshaw Trade Association to be responsible for distribution. The association and others will guarantee that they will not request additional licenses, etc. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities has reported this to the municipal government and ordered the Rickshaw Trade Association to comply and properly distribute the licenses, it is said.

Family of Three Found Dead from Coal Gas Poisoning in Yongxiang Lane, Zhabei: Pan Jinchang and Sons Dafu and Xiaofu Die Simultaneously; Coal Gas Poisoning Confirmed 155

At 53 Yongxiang Lane, Datong Road, Zhabei, a three-room tenant named Pan Jinchang, who had just moved in three days prior, had two sons named Dafu, about twenty years old, and Xiaofu, eighteen years old this year. The father and sons usually made a living by steaming and selling steamed buns. For many years, they had been setting up their stall near the Xiaocai market in front of the Samsung Teahouse. They had recently moved to Yongxiang Lane. Every night, they would close their stall at two or three in the morning. Unexpectedly, after closing the stall around 2 a.m. the night before, the coal stove used for steaming buns was not extinguished. Dafu and his younger brother slept on a small bed along the window, while Pan Jinchang slept on the floor. At the time, the doors and windows were tightly closed. After falling asleep, the father and sons all died from coal gas poisoning due to their hard work during the day. When dawn broke, the neighbors did not see them getting up and suspected that they were resting at home due to their hard work in recent days. At 11:30 a.m., a friend of Pan's named Liu Bingwen went to Pan's residence and, seeing that Pan had not yet gotten up, shouted loudly, but there was no response, raising suspicions. Liu then summoned police officer Quan Jiugao from Post No. 11 of the 4th District Public Security Bureau to come and help the landlord Sha Guifeng (46 years old, local, electrician) open the windows and doors. To their shock, all three had already died. The police officer immediately reported to police chief Yuan Pilie, who reported to the 4th District and then to Lu Abao, the district chief of the 11th Ward. They reported to the Shanghai Local Court to request an autopsy. Yesterday afternoon at around 3 p.m., prosecutor Xiao Jinying and others were dispatched to the scene. The autopsy confirmed that the deceased Pan Jinchang, son Dafu, and son Xiaofu had indeed died from coal gas poisoning. The coroner's report was filled out, and the district chief was instructed to arrange for the collection of the bodies. Because the deceased had family in their hometown, a telegram was sent to Zhenjiang by the deceased's relatives and friends to summon their family members to Shanghai, it is said.

Teacher Convicted of Raping Female Student: Sentenced to Six Years and Two Months in Prison 156

Li Xizhi, a teacher at Shangde Elementary School, was accused by Gu Zhangshi, the mother of female student Gu Cuizhen, of seducing and raping Cuizhen and instigating Cuizhen to steal more than forty yuan to pay for hotel expenses. She also stated that Cuizhen was seventeen years old and had not yet reached the age of sixteen, which constituted rape under criminal law. Therefore, the prosecutor filed a public prosecution based on the victim's statement. During the criminal court hearing, Li Xizhi presented evidence to the contrary, including the hotel's revolving ledger, which indicated that Cuizhen had written her age as eighteen and that she had not been sleeping with him; rather, she had opened the hotel room herself, and there was no seduction. However, the trial judge found that the evidence presented by Li Xizhi could not be adopted. Therefore, yesterday's verdict was that Li Xizhi was sentenced to six years of imprisonment for raping a girl under the age of sixteen and four months of imprisonment for instigating theft, to be served concurrently as six years and two months, and deprived of public rights for seven years. However, Li, being dissatisfied with this verdict, naturally appealed, and the court ordered that an appeal was permissible. He was then returned to custody.

Japanese Mail Ship Lushan Maru; Signs of Pirates Discovered; Sailed Back to Wusongkou; Thorough Search Yielded Nothing Overnight 167

-Ten People with Suspicious Behavior Captured-

Yesterday, the Japanese Shanghai Daily reported that the Lushan Maru, belonging to the Nissin Kisen Kaisha, departed for Guangdong at 1:00 p.m. On the 1st. At 6:00 p.m., when leaving the Wusongkou, it was suddenly discovered that pirates disguised as passengers had mixed into the ship. The captain, Tominaga, immediately telegraphed the Nissin Kisen Kaisha by wireless, stating, "There is danger among the passengers, return to Shanghai on the same ship." The company was greatly shocked upon receiving the telegram and immediately reported the telegram's content to the police department of the Consulate General. The police department prepared a small boat at the Hongkou Wharf to wait. At 8:30 p.m., the Lushan Maru entered the port. At 9:00 p.m., the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and twenty members of the police department of the Consulate General, all wearing bulletproof vests, along with the branch manager of the ship's company, Mr. Yamanaka, and supervisor Asai, went to the Pudong Wharf for inspection. Because there were eighty Chinese third-class passengers on board and a large amount of cargo was loaded, the Japanese Consulate General dispatched twenty-five police officers and the Public Security Bureau dispatched fifty police officers, who boarded the Lushan Maru on small boats and inspected the bodies of the eighty Chinese passengers one by one. Until 11:00 p.m., no weapons were found. However, eight people who behaved suspiciously were arrested first. Later, the luggage was thoroughly searched overnight, but no weapons were found until 3:00 a.m. It was also heard that during the inspection of the third-class passengers of the Lushan Maru, two more suspects were found. These people detected that the ship was carrying artificial silk and other goods worth 200,000 taels that day. Because the ship suddenly sailed back, they may have thrown weapons into the sea to destroy evidence, which is also unknown.

Selling Enemy Goods - Wooden Combs; Actually Made in Nagasaki, Falsely Labeled "Made in Germany"; Trademark "Camel" is the Same as That of the American Asian Company - Asian American Company Files a Lawsuit 171

Yang Songmei from Suzhou used to operate Yang Yongtai Silver Mirror Shop at 4 Liangshan Lane, Rue Pére Robert, French Concession, but has now moved to 1 Yuancheng Lane, Avenue Lafayette. Yang also sells wooden combs from the enemy country. The wooden combs are manufactured by Suzuka Shotenl in Nagasaki, Japan, but are falsely labeled as "Made in Germany" to deceive the people of the country. The trademark used is completely the same as the "Camel" trademark of the American Asian Company. The selling price is much cheaper than the Asian American product, resulting in thriving business and considerable profits. Recently, the Asian American Company learned of this and first went to Wanxiang Sock Factory at 188 Yunnan Road, a reseller, and purchased two defective wooden combs. They immediately reported to the Laoza Police Department, who ordered Chinese detective Zhang Yuanjing, investigator Pang Ruiqing, and Western detective Kladen to rush to Wanxiang and seize three dozen and two more pieces of counterfeit goods. According to Wanxiang's confession, they went to Yang Yongtai Shop and arrested Yang and the street vendor Zhu Zhishao from Suzhou, and seized a total of more than 4,200 enemy wooden combs of various sizes, and took them back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the 2nd Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Lawyer Qian Xunjiu of the police department stated the facts of the case and filed a public prosecution under Article 268 of the Criminal Code, stating that more than 20 invoices for sales were also seized from the defendant, all stamped with the return receipts of various merchants. The police are currently investigating, and whether to prosecute Wanxiang Shop is also under consideration.

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau has decided to offer special preferential measures for passengers to facilitate travel to scenic spots along the two railway lines: (1) Add special tourist express trains to Shanghai-Wuxi and Shanghai-Hangzhou on weekends. The train to Hangzhou departs from Shanghai at 12:35 p.m. on Saturday noon and returns the following evening. (3) Strive for comfortable seating and thoughtful service. (4) There are extremely light restrictions to avoid overcrowding, but non-tourists can still ride the train with special express train tickets. People in Shanghai who have lived in the bustling dust for a long time rely on travel to regulate their tense lives. Everyone who hears about this move by the Railway Bureau praises it.

German Cultural Groups Hold Concert of Ancient Chinese Poetry 181

The Shanghai Chinese-German Association and the East Asian Society, two German groups, are scheduled to hold a concert of ancient Chinese poetry at the Lyceum Theatre on Mailly Road in the French Concession at 9:15 p.m. on May 3rd. It is noted that Chinese and Western music are fundamentally different in principle. Therefore, if ancient Chinese poems are translated into German, set to Western music, and sung, while at the same time the original Chinese text is also accompanied by Chinese instruments and sung, two completely different results can be obtained for comparison. Although the translation strives not to lose the original meaning, Chinese and Western poets cannot have the same concept of emotion, and when it is set to Western music, it feels even more different. This concert of ancient Chinese poetry aims to express this difference. The entire program includes more than ten ancient poems, which are works by famous Chinese writers throughout history, such as Li Bai's "Hearing the Flute in Luoyang on a Cold Night," Tao Yuanming's "When Sunflowers Bloom," Bai Juyi's "Remembering the Willows on the River," and Wang Han's "Liangzhou Ci," which is "Grape Wine and Night-Shining Cups." Finally, there will be an excerpt from "The Story of the Pipa." For example, for the poem "Hearing the Flute in Luoyang on a Cold Night," the translation will be sung with Western music first, and then Mr. Chen Dajun will sing the original text solo, accompanied by the pipa, erhu, and flute. Listeners can see that Chinese music does not have polyphony or harmony, and the instruments play the same tones as the singing, supporting the spirit of the singing. The interludes before and after are where the emotions of the entire song are placed. All the beauty of Chinese music lies in this. When Mr. Chen Dajun sings, he will also appear on stage in ancient costume, so its touching effect will be even more profound. As for the translation, due to the aforementioned differences in the emotions of Chinese and Western poets, the translator's response after being inspired by the original poem has become another realm. If the translator sticks to the original meaning and seeks only to be faithful, he must sacrifice his own poetic meaning. Therefore, the beauty of the translation has already become a purely Western flavor, which is then combined with the harmony of Western music and slightly mixed with Chinese colors, making people unable to help but feel leisurely and fascinated. From this, it can be seen that Chinese and Western music are each an entity, and if they are presented in a pure style, they can better enable people to understand than those who imitate each other and mix them into a chapter. The initiative of the Chinese-German Association and the East Asian Society is not only to encourage the study of ancient Chinese poetry.

Establishment of the Chinese Aeronautical Engineering Society 182

Chinese aviation organizations, such as the Aviation Association of Beiping, the Chinese Aviation Comrades Association of Nanjing, the Chinese Aviation Promotion Association of Shanghai, and the current Chinese Aviation Association, are all public propaganda groups. In addition, the Aviation Society of Beiping, the Flying Association, and the Flying Club of Shanghai are similar to club organizations for aviation enthusiasts. There has been a lack of initiators for genuine aeronautical academic organizations. The reason for this is due to the lack of domestic experts and the backwardness of aviation. Recently, technicians working at the Hangzhou Aviation Agency held a meeting to organize the Chinese Aeronautical Engineering Society, and Zhu Lin, Guo Lisan, and Li Lide were appointed as drafters of the constitution. They sent letters to various aviation engineering experts in the country to solicit opinions. Those who agreed to serve as sponsors included senior technicians from the Military Affairs Commission, the Aviation Administration, and its affiliated Central Aviation School and various repair factories and aviation teams, as well as more than 40 aviation engineering experts who studied in Europe and the United States from China Airlines, Eurasia Airlines, the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Office, the Hunan Aviation Office, Central University, Tsinghua University, and Zhejiang University. The inaugural meeting was held at the Hangzhou Aviation Administration Office on April 1st, the constitution was approved, and seven directors were elected. Among the directors, Qian Changzuo, Director of the Technical Department of the Aviation Administration, was elected as Chairman, Nie Kaiyi, Deputy Director of the Flight Group of China Airlines, as Vice Chairman, and Wang Chenfu, Factory Director of the Central Aviation School Factory, as Secretary-General. Liu Jingyi, Factory Director of the Capital Aviation Factory of the Aviation Administration, Zhu Lin, Head of the Equipment and Materials Section, Jiang Chaoxi, Professor of Central University, and Guo Lisan, Education Officer of the Central Aviation School, were elected as directors. The main work of the Society is the organization of academic research associations, divided into groups such as air, dynamics, aircraft design, engines, airships and balloons, factory management, aircraft maintenance, aviation materials, aviation terminology, and aviation meteorology. Each member must choose at least one group to participate in the work. At present, most of the groups have been prepared and plan to hold an annual meeting within this year to publicly discuss the research results of each group. The Society has also begun to submit applications to the Ministry of Education and the Military Affairs Commission for registration, and it will make considerable contributions to the development of Chinese aviation in the future.

A Rare Song Dynasty Edition of Buddhist Scriptures 183

The Song Dynasty Qisha Edition of the Great Buddhist Canon is a rare and exquisite edition from 700 years ago, which is extremely convenient for the four assemblies to recite, study, and research. The first batch of 50 volumes has now been published, with a total of 329 scriptures in 616 volumes. It is a printed version from the Duanping, Jiaxi, and Chunyou periods of the Song Lizong era, and some were added as supplements during the Dade period of the Yuan Dynasty, which is very solemn and exquisite. Resident Zhao Yunchang of the Nantong Baochang, and his son Zongyi, deeply believe in Buddhism. They specially purchased a copy from the Song Edition Sutra Reprinting Society at No. 714 Weihaiwei Road in this city to provide and offer. The entire scripture consists of more than 6,000 volumes and is exquisitely printed from the original version, costing only more than 500 yuan. It is needed by those who lecture on versions, those who study Chinese culture and history, and those who appreciate Buddhist art. For oneself, one has already accomplished this pure wish, and also leave this pure wish to be passed on to future generations. The joy felt in this spirit is incomparable to other kinds of books. Venerable Master Yin Guang has been invited to write a preface to record this event, the original text of which is as follows: Zhao Yunchang of Nantong Baochang Town has inherited family virtues for generations, passed down through farming and reading, only cultivating heavenly nobility, not admiring worldly glory, deeply believing in cause and effect, and earnestly cultivating pure karma. Desiring to have his children and grandchildren forever keep and replace these virtues, he has specially requested the Song Edition Great Buddhist Canon to be offered in the family Buddhist hall, in order to have his children and grandchildren, as well as all members of the clan, be able to receive, uphold, read, and recite it, so as not to be born in vain and die in vain. He prays that Guang will write a preface to show it to future generations. Now, because the Yuan Yin Song Collection Association has ordered Guang to write a preface, I will copy its original text and briefly describe Mr. Zhao's deep love for his children, grandchildren, and clansmen. May those who see and hear this immediately put it into practice according to their own abilities, and do not just act like fools who have arrived at the Treasure Mountain and still return empty-handed. Then not only will they not disappoint the Buddha's transformation and not betray their own spirits, but they can also greatly comfort Mr. Zhao's earnest intention in requesting the scriptures.

Refutation of the Rent Increase Case at Jing'an Villa 188

The houses at Jing'an Villa on Jing'an Temple Road are managed by Hua Ji Company, and the rents are already very high. At the end of last year, the landlord suddenly notified the tenants along the street that the rents would be re-priced from January of this year, and tenants who wish to renew their leases must sign a new lease contract, etc. Upon hearing the news, the tenants all knew that the purpose of this move was nothing more than to increase the rent. However, due to the extreme economic depression in this city, they were unable to bear the rent increase and sent representatives to negotiate, but without any results. The landlord, dissatisfied with the failure to increase the rent, used the excuse of taking back the property for his own use and first filed a lawsuit against the Kaiser Restaurant on the premises, requesting the First Special District Local Court to order them to move out and declare provisional execution. The restaurant was very angry at the landlord's oppression and requested assistance from the Rent Reduction Committee. The Committee entrusted its legal counsel, Lawyer Sun Biwu, to appear in court to argue the case on its behalf. Lawyer Sun collected evidence to prove the landlord's intention was not to take back the house for his own use and vigorously refuted it based on the law. The case was recently ruled on yesterday, and the plaintiff's claim was dismissed.

Inspection Reports of Two Banks 191

The Central Bank's 195th Inspection Report on Issuance Reserves states that, in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, the Bank is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the issuance of convertible banknotes. The 195th inspection was held at the Bank's Issuance Bureau on April 30th, 1934, and the results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible banknotes issued is 69,319,270 silver dollars, including 62,922,869 silver dollar banknotes and 6,396,401 subsidiary coin banknotes. The total amount of the convertible banknote reserve fund is 69,319,270 silver dollars, including 56,293,270 silver dollars in cash reserves. This cash reserve includes 52,820,113 yuan stored in the Bank's Issuance Treasury, 1,700,696 yuan stored in branch banks in various ports, and 1,772,461 yuan stored in correspondent banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 13,026,000 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of Customs Gold convertible banknotes issued is 373,324.70 yuan, and the total amount of the Customs Gold convertible banknote reserve fund is 373,324.70 yuan. This reserve fund includes 7,351.95 taels of standard gold, which is converted to 373,324.70 Customs Gold at a fixed price of 0.50779. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The inspection results show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%. The numbers are consistent with the regulations, and this report is made accordingly. May 1, 1934, Li Fusun, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank; Supervisors Xie Mingxun, Zhen Songsun, Tai Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Jiqing.

The China General Chamber of Commerce Bank's Issuance Reserve Inspection Report states that the issuance of convertible banknotes and reserve funds of the China General Chamber of Commerce Bank for April 1934 have now been inspected by Supervisors Chuan Qilin, He Shaoyin, and Xie Jishan, together with Accountant Xu Yongzuo, on May 1st. The results of the inspection are listed as follows: The total amount of convertible banknotes issued is 17,249,100 yuan, and the total amount of the reserve fund is 17,249,100 yuan, including a cash reserve of 12,496,600 yuan (over 60%) and a guarantee reserve of 4,752,500 yuan (over 40%). The numbers are in accordance with the issuance regulations.

Weather Report 199

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather in Northeast China and Shandong is unstable with blowing sand. The wind is from the southwest to the northwest and is quite strong due to the passage of a Mongolian low pressure system moving east or southeast-east. The Yangtze River Basin and the area around here will change from sunny to cloudy with haze or drizzle. The wind is from the southeast to the southwest and is quite strong. The coastal area south of Ma'an Island is cloudy with strong winds from the northeast to the east. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city was a maximum of 73.0 and a minimum of 47.1. On the same day last year, the maximum was 65.8 and the minimum was 62.6.

To the Editor,

I read the news item in the Local News section of your newspaper on April 27th about the drug den seized in Dunren Lane, Wangzhi Road. It mentioned a person named Sun Peisheng working at the Central European store, etc. Upon investigation, Sun Peisheng had already left at the end of last year and has no relationship with our store. The statement in your newspaper that Sun Peisheng was arrested at our store is a misunderstanding. We hereby send this letter to clarify and request a correction.

Sincerely,

Central European Pharmacy

To the Editor,

After reading the news item in the Local News section of your newspaper on May 1st about the love suicide case of Yang Binghu and Chen Zhujun, it stated that the prostitute Yifei was released from her contract by Xie Peide, the manager of the China Cement Company. It concerns our reputation, so we specially sent this letter to inform you and hope that you will make a serious correction to show the truth.

Sincerely,

China Cement Co., Ltd.

Our National Athletes Set Off on the Country's Journey: Aboard the McKinley Steamer Bound for the Philippines, Yesterday's Flag-Granting Ceremony Held at the Municipal Government: Farewell, Gentlemen, Have a Safe Journey 202

The Chinese delegation to the 10th Far Eastern Games set sail for the Philippines today aboard the McKinley steamer. They boarded the ship at the Shanghai Customs Wharf on the Bund at Sanma Road at 1:30 PM. The athletes, totaling 142, include football, swimming, and Hong Kong and Guangdong volleyball and baseball players, who will gather when the ship arrives in Hong Kong and travel to the Philippines together. Ms. Gao Zi, the head coach of the women's team, is said to be unable to travel to the Philippines due to busy official duties. Advisor Topping (Director General of the YMCA Sports Department) and four shooting athletes are all self-funded. Yesterday at noon, all the athletes in Shanghai gathered at the Municipal Government where Mayor Wu held a flag-granting ceremony. After the ceremony, there was a gathering and meal at the Municipal Government. The details are as follows:
