Mayor Wu Grants the Flag (Photo by Wang Kai)

Flag-Granting Ceremony 206

The Chinese delegation to the 10th Far Eastern Games, due to their imminent departure, was specially invited by Mayor Wu Tiecheng of this city to a banquet for all staff and athletes at the Municipal Government in the city center at 1:00 PM yesterday, and a flag-granting ceremony was held. The details are as follows:

Full Participation: Around 12:00 noon yesterday, all staff and athletes participating in the Far Eastern Games gathered at the YMCA in Baxianqiao. Li Dachao, the chief of the First Section of the Municipal Government, hired more than ten cars to transport all staff and athletes to the Municipal Government in the city center. After a brief rest in the reception room of the Municipal Government, the flag-granting ceremony was held in front of the Municipal Government Auditorium.

Ceremony Order: The order of the flag-granting ceremony was as follows: (1) All stand at attention, (2) Sing the Party Song, (3) Pay the highest respects to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Premier, (4) The Mayor respectfully reads the Premier's will, (5) Silence, (6) The Mayor delivers a speech, (7) Flag presentation: A. National Flag, B. Athletes' Team Flag (8) Athletes' representative gives a thank you speech, (9) Photography, (10) Luncheon

Photo of the Chinese athletes attending the Far East Games (International Photography Society)

Mayor's Speech: After the ceremony was completed, Mayor Wu delivered a speech, stating that he was extremely honored to have representatives and athletes from the Sports Association. Today, he was presenting the flag to the delegation attending the Far Eastern Games, wishing them to bring glory to the country and the nation under the shining light of the national flag and the team flag and return with honor. The honor of the Chinese delegation is the honor of China, which is what the people of the whole country expect from them and wish them to be awarded. He wished them victory.

Representative Accepts: After the Mayor's speech, the flag presentation was held. Zhang Lingjia, the captain of the track and field team, was chosen to accept the national flag, and Tang Baokun, the captain of the basketball team, accepted the team flag. The national flag was the one prepared for the Chinese athletes to participate in the World Games held in the United States the year before last. The team flag had a blue satin background with black velvet characters reading "Chinese Delegation to the 10th Far Eastern Games" in horizontal stripes. In the middle was the "Sports" character in seal script, and below was the inscription "Presented by Wu Tiecheng," also cut from black velvet.

Luncheon Held: The original item of the athletes' representative giving a thank you speech was omitted due to time constraints. Therefore, after the flag presentation, a photograph was taken in front of the auditorium. After the photography was completed, Mayor Wu personally hosted a luncheon in the dining hall of the Municipal Government. All staff and athletes enjoyed themselves until 1:30 PM before dispersing.

Wang Zhengting Speaks: Wang Zhengting, Chairman of the National Sports Association, went to Nanjing to meet with President Wang to discuss various issues related to attending the Far Eastern Games. He returned to Shanghai the night before last after completing his official duties and is scheduled to lead the Chinese athletes aboard the McKinley President Steamer of the Da Lai Company this afternoon to attend the Far Eastern Games. Regarding Wang's visit to Nanjing to meet with President Wang, there has been much speculation from the Japanese side, and it has been said that Wang will take on a certain important position. Wang formally denied this statement yesterday.

Hao Gengsheng Completes Inspection, Arrives in Shanghai, and Departs for the Philippines 207

Hao Gengsheng, a sports supervisor from the Ministry of Education, inspected the sports activities of schools in the provinces of Pingjin, Bian, Xiang, and Lu for more than fifty days, which was quite arduous. He also solicited 3,000 yuan from He Jian, Liu Zhi, and Shen Honglie to fund the Far Eastern Games. The 45,000 yuan in aid from the Ministry of Education was also facilitated by Hao. He arrived in Shanghai early to assist the Sports Association and is departing for the Philippines today to attend the Far Eastern Games.

The Philippines Actively Prepares for the Far Eastern Games: Work on the Stadium is Being Rushed 208

(Dispatch from the Japanese News Agency Correspondent in Manila on the 30th) The opening date of the Far Eastern Games is approaching within ten days. The various competition venues at the Games site are ready, but the volleyball and basketball courts have not yet been completed and are currently being rushed. The baseball field is quite magnificent and can accommodate 18,000 spectators. The command post of the track and field stadium has been completed, and temporary stands are currently being built around it, with a total of 20,000 seats. Filipino athletes are already practicing in the swimming pool, and the stands have also been 80% completed. At the Dilasai University, where athletes from China, Japan, and the Philippines are staying together, 160 Filipino athletes are staying and are undergoing rigorous training daily under strict supervision. The athletes' dormitories are too narrow to accommodate all the athletes, so some of the Chinese athletes will be housed elsewhere. The Games Preparatory Committee is currently rushing to make mosquito nets for the athletes.

Kaitai Cup Final Game Ends in a Draw - Final Rematch on the 9th of This Month 216

The Kaitai Cup final game between China and England against Five Continents has been postponed twice. On the 29th, it rained again. Because Mr. Xiang Songmao, the former general manager of Five Continents, passed away yesterday and today, the team members will attend the funeral in Ningbo. Therefore, with the consent of both parties, it was changed to be held yesterday morning at the football field. Referee Mr. Shen Huichun, Mr. Cao Qiuting, and Mr. Li Baojun served as line judges. Because this game is related to the outcome of the championship, the two teams fought fiercely. In the first half, in a tense atmosphere, Cheng Likang of Five Continents got a good opportunity and scored a goal with a powerful kick, opening the record. In the second half, China and England, after being wounded, counterattacked deep into the opponent's territory, and Wu Yinling scored successfully, making the score 1-1, resulting in a draw. According to practice, the game was extended for 20 minutes, but neither side achieved anything. After agreement by both teams, it was decided to hold a rematch at 7:00 AM on the 9th of this month at the football field. The lineups of the two teams yesterday are listed below:

Various competitions will be held at the Chinese Athletics Field on Father Lao Shen Road starting at 2:00 PM in the afternoon. In addition to the football and basketball championships, and the bicycle race, which will be held outdoors at 8:00 AM on the 4th (route attached separately) in advance, all other competitions will be held on the 5th and 6th. The details of each item are listed below:

Bicycle Race The participants include six groups: Great Northern Telegraph Bureau, Great Eastern Telegraph Bureau, International Wireless Radio Station, Pacific Telegraph Bureau, China Telegraph Bureau, and the Postal Workers' Union. They are scheduled to gather before 8:00 AM on May 4th at Bridge No. 2, Qimei Road, Disiwei Road. Before the race, the vehicles must be inspected. It is stipulated that all use eighteen-person gear double-fly bicycles. Each group may send six athletes. The first four to arrive can represent the group and score points (for example, the first to arrive gets one point, the second to arrive gets two points, and so on). The group with the lowest score among the four people will be the champion team. Boy Scouts will maintain order along the way, and there will be inspectors at the turnaround point to record the numbers. The route is as follows: Start from Bridge No. 2, Qimei Road, heading northeast to the Second Sub-bureau of the Seventh District Public Security Bureau, turn east to Xiangyin Road to Guohe Road, head north past the Qiu Jiang Bridge and the First Park to the end of Guohe Road, loop back along the original route to Bridge No. 2, Qimei Road, as the finish line. The distance is approximately 10,600 meters.

Competition Items There are two types: scoring championships and performances. The championships are divided into football, basketball, tennis, track and field. The performances are divided into women's track events, martial arts, table tennis, race walking, bicycles, and group exercises. The track and field events are as follows: (1) 100 meters, (2) 200 meters, (3) 400 meters, (5) 800 meters, (6) 1500 meters, (7) 3000 meters, (8) 200 meters low hurdles (9) 800 meters relay, (10) 12-pound shot put, (11) discus, (12) javelin, (13) high jump, (14) long jump, (15) pole vault.

Education News from Other Places

Key Points for Improving Education in Henan Province - Report from the Ministry of Education Supervisor 219

The Ministry of Education previously sent supervisor Zhou Bangdao to inspect education in Henan Province. The results of the inspection have been reported to the Ministry of Education. The key points for improving education in Henan are now explored as follows:

(1) The province's education funding has long been independent, but the management methods should be strictly guarded in the future to avoid fluctuations. (2) Provincial secondary schools are mostly concentrated in larger cities along the Longhai and Pinghan railways, while the western corner of Henan is extremely sparse. This distribution is very uneven. Future establishment of secondary schools should pay attention to adjustment. (3) Normal school districts should be designated immediately to set up various normal schools separately. The number of classes in each school should also be properly regulated according to actual needs to avoid the problem of oversupply or overdemand of teachers in a certain area. (4) The entire province has no vocational schools for women, and remedies should be planned urgently. (5) Subsidies for private secondary schools are granted according to the level of achievement, which is considered fair. However, the amount of funding for each school should be appropriately adjusted based on the number of classes. (6) The number of county-level normal schools in each county is still considerable, but the content is often lacking, and the graduation years vary. Improvements should be made in accordance with the regulations for normal schools. (7) The salaries of principals of provincial secondary schools are measured by the number of classes, which is considered fair. However, academic qualifications and experience should also be used as standards. Also, the salaries of teachers in secondary schools are generally calculated by clock hours, and the full-time system has not been implemented, which is not appropriate and should be immediately formulated by the Ministry of Secondary School Teachers and Staff Salary Scales and Annual Salary Increase Methods for approval. (8) The distribution of county-level elementary schools in each county is uneven, and the amount of elementary schools in towns and villages is too small. School names have not been revised in accordance with elementary school regulations and should be improved separately. (9) Many counties have drafted plans for the implementation of compulsory education, but there are many who hesitate to observe or fail to implement them vigorously. Strict supervision should be immediately imposed to ensure widespread implementation as soon as possible. (10) There are still independent senior elementary schools in each county, which is inappropriate and should be ordered to add junior elementary schools or merge with other local junior elementary schools. (11) Provincial elementary schools that are piloting the two-part system have encountered difficulties due to insufficient preparation in advance. They should be ordered to conduct in-depth research and improvement and appropriately increase funding to facilitate distribution. (12) The Children's Science Museum established by the Kaifeng Experimental Zone Committee has gathered various scientific equipment for use by elementary schools throughout the city. This method is quite economical and appropriate, and should be imitated in other places to solve the problem of relatively difficult teaching equipment. (13) Social education funding, regardless of provincial or county funds, is far from the standards set by the Ministry of Education. A comprehensive plan should be immediately made to allocate a portion of the new funding to social education so that social education can gradually progress with school education, without fear of imbalance. (14) Staff of social education institutions in various counties often lack in-depth research and progressive spirit in social education, resulting in mediocre results and loss of social trust. They should be cultivated and carefully appointed in the future. (15) The Henan Provincial Production Education Implementation Plan, the Henan Provincial Public Education Implementation Plan, and the Henan Health Education Implementation Plan formulated by the Education Department are relevant in content and should be implemented seriously in accordance with them. (16) Shangcheng, Huangchuan, and other counties in the southern Henan Special Zone have been recovered for a long time. They should be quickly subjected to universal special training in accordance with the Education Facilities Plan of the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Special Zone.

Ye Suizhong Takes Over as New Director of Education in Zhejiang 220

Mr. Ye Suizhong, the newly appointed Provincial Committee member and Director of the Education Department of Zhejiang Province, arrived at the department at 8:00 AM on the 1st, accompanied by Li Zhenxia, Section Chief of the Fourth Section of the Education Department, to take over. Zhao Jiyu, the original acting head of the Third Section, remained in the position of instructor. Secretary He Jinghuang was reassigned to the position of supervisor. Except for Guo Yisun of the First Section, Zheng Tonghua of the Third Section, and Shen Fuhou of the Fourth Section, whose future appointments are pending, the other old staff members will not be changed. Regarding the overall education plan, Mr. Ye mainly follows the old rules without any changes.

Local News

City Education Bureau Holds Elementary School Arithmetic Competition - Yesterday Ordered Schools to Expedite 222

The City Education Bureau of this city issued an order yesterday to the municipal and registered private elementary schools regarding the scheduled arithmetic competition for elementary schools:

The types and dates of gatherings to be held this semester have been notified in advance. The elementary school arithmetic competition is scheduled to be held in early May. Now that the scheduled date is approaching, the schools should be ordered to abide by the following points and expedite the competition. (1) The scope of this competition will temporarily be the level of grades four and six of elementary school, divided into two groups. (2) The competition procedure is divided into three stages: preliminary round, semi-final round, and final round. The preliminary round will be organized by the schools themselves, and the semi-final round will be held by district. The final round will be held by the city. The topics for these rounds will be set by the bureau and staff will be assigned to preside over them. (3) Each school in the preliminary round will select three outstanding representatives from each group (six in total) and complete the competition before May 4. The names should be listed separately and reported to the bureau in order to participate in the semi-final round. The semi-final round is scheduled to be held on May 15. The number of candidates admitted will be one-tenth of the total number of candidates admitted to the preliminary round in each district, in each group, to participate in the final round. The date of the final round will be determined after the semi-final round is completed. (4) The judges for the semi-final round will be separately hired by the bureau, and the evaluation standards will be specified separately. (5) The venue and time for the semi-final round will be notified separately. The semi-final round exam papers will be prepared and issued by the bureau. (6) Those admitted to the semi-final round will be given prizes by the bureau according to the results and grades.

Spring and Autumn

A Record of Incense Drifting by the Imperial Court 225

— Originally Written by Princess Der Ling of Qing, Translated by Qin Shouou

As long as they did not see anyone sitting down alone in the carriages - including the coal shoveler on the coal pile - and no brakeman moving on the yellow carriage tops without permission, they considered their mission accomplished. However, even such simple tasks were exhausting enough for them because they had to watch constantly and could not sit down.

Here, let me tell you a few more detailed situations.

Meng Fuxiang certainly had one or two important assistants, although he himself did nothing at all. How could these assistants assist? But since he was a more important senior official, he always had several assistants as usual. And these assistants also had assistants with them. So there were many of them. This situation had become an unchangeable custom in the Manchu Qing officialdom for hundreds of years. Whenever a person got an official position where he could make a lot of money, he had to bring all the men in his family with him and let them occupy various important assistant positions. Therefore, if you want these people to actually do something for the country or the people with the money they took, it is as impossible as a rooster laying eggs!

Meng Fuxiang! Now dead for many years! He was the director of the Jingfeng Railway at that time.

The only thing he did was the inflow and outflow of money. Although on the surface he was appointed by the Empress Dowager, if someone caught the chief eunuch Li Lianying and forced him to tell the truth with cruel punishment, we would know that Meng Fuxiang's position was completely bought from Li Lianying by spending a huge amount of money on lobbying. (24)

The Use of Women 226

— Chen Liang

In the past two or three days, I have either strolled on the road, or wandered in the park, or "prepared tea and snacks" and invited girlfriends to conduct a personal investigation. I have gained a lot of insights into the use of women.

One day, the weather was very good, and there were many photographers in the park. The dead trees and the dull rocks had neither curved beauty nor charming potential. Therefore, those who brought cameras must bring women, either sitting and laughing, lying down and happy, looking up at the clouds, or lowering their heads to peel sesame bananas and the like. They could all be photographed. Their postures were natural, which could not be matched by the dead things like trees and stones. "If there were no women in the world, there would be no invention of the camera." I can believe this if I measure it by reason.

One day, I had no side dishes to drink, so I went to buy a hundred strings of Sichuan pickles and spread them on the table, drinking and humming "Peach Blossom River is a Beauty's Nest." The landlady's daughter came either because she heard the singing or smelled the alcohol. "How much is this pack of pickles?" "One hundred coins!" "I can buy it for only fifty coins." So she gave her five copper coins and bought another pack, which was indeed "better than the previous one." At this point, I suddenly exclaimed, "May all the 'bargains' in the world belong to women."

One day, I put on a bamboo cloth robe and went to XX alma mater to see the art exhibition, but was stopped at the ticket office. "I am an old alumnus!" "I don't recognize you." I asked the principal to come out to recognize me. "Hey! You're quite pretentious." They ignored me. After a moment, three female students came, followed by two men, dressed in Western suits. "Tickets for these two gentlemen." "Make believe." The female student squinted and said. The ticket seller said again, "Public affairs must be handled impartially." "Never mind, never mind." - Three women and two men crowded in, and I could only sigh at the school gate.

Although the above are small matters, aren't they the "usefulness" of "women"?

"The use of women is indeed great!"

Travel Companions 227

— Jinxi

By some chance, I had a trip to Yiwu. You may not know this small county in Zhejiang Province, so I must explain that it is located in the middle of the Hangjiang Road. The historical figures Zong Ze and Luo Binwang, two loyal ministers who planned for the country, were born there.

I took the third express train from Xixing, Hangzhou, at 6:00 PM and arrived in Yiwu at 12:00 AM. It took six hours to sit in the car for a quarter of a day and night. But this time I didn't yawn or fall asleep in the car. The reason is that I was lucky enough to have several travel companions: those naive children and that row of naive and friendly soldiers. They could hum tunes and say silly things with laughter, entertaining not only themselves but also others. They themselves were art.

Art is produced around those who have not been educated and whose minds are too simple to think about the unknowable future with patience. University professors object to writing rickshaw pullers into novels, and aesthetic artists advocate discovering art around women who sway their bodies like snakes. I think there are some mistakes. Friends, this row of soldiers, they don't know that they are dozens of human bombs. They don't want to speculate on the end of their lives and the places where they will be buried. If a writer pierces their minds with a pen and conveys them in detail, making a novel, its value will not be lower than Turgenev's "A Sportsman's Sketches."

Thanks to the soldiers, they were my travel companions, guiding my artistic view to the other side of life.

The Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 228

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Eight: A Coincidence at the Theater, A Fool Picks Up a Handkerchief out of Infatuation. Diligent Inquiries about Illness, Misunderstanding from a Letter.

Madam Jiang, listening from the side, fully understood the situation and replied with a smile, "Yes, Old Master, your behavior is much like that celestial official on the stage." Old Master Zhao shook his head with a smile, "How can that be compared?" Madam Jiang laughed, "Why can't it be compared? Your thoughtfulness towards your daughter-in-law is perhaps even better than that celestial official." As she said this, Guizhi turned her head towards Old Master Zhao with a smile, following the tone of her words. This turn of her head brought her face to face with Ji Zhi. Though her smile was not directed at Ji Zhi, the sight of it stirred his heart nonetheless. He knew that with her father-in-law and mother-in-law present, he must not let his thoughts wander, so he kept his gaze fixed on the stage. However, though his eyes were on the stage, his nose could detect scents from all directions. As he steadied himself, focusing intently on the stage, he was constantly assailed by waves of fragrance. After being struck by the scent for a long time, Ji Zhi looked ahead and saw only men in blue cloth clothing. Behind him, there were two women with oily black hair and heavily powdered faces, so vulgar they were repulsive; they would not be the source of any fragrance. That meant the scent must be coming from Guizhi. Though Guizhi had lightly applied some powder to her face, it did not seem like high-quality makeup, so it shouldn't be emitting any fragrance. Then, where was this fragrance coming from? As Ji Zhi was pondering this question, he glanced sideways at Guizhi. However, it was only a fleeting moment, as he was afraid that his improper behavior might displease the two old people. In reality, the two old people didn't seem to notice anything, but Guizhi was secretly anxious. She thought to herself, "How could I be so careless, sitting so close to him? He keeps glancing around; I must not let the old master see this behavior." (3751)

A Rude Awakening 229

— Shi Ying

The Monroe Cake of Asia

Old 230

— A Shock

A Qing used to be my brave warrior, when I shouldered a gun and carried a leather bag, he would always follow me closely.

Every time a bird fell after being struck by my bullet, A Qing would bravely and fiercely extend his iron legs and run forward, quickly bringing the captured prey to me in his mouth. A Qing was indeed my trusted and brave follower. Now A Qing is old, he can no longer be as lively and fierce as before, what he now has is very, very slow steps, old and sparse barks, hair loss, and gluttony, all characteristics of old age.

"Go! You old thing!" Children often hit and kick him when they are unhappy, venting their depression. Alas! Who would have dared to bully him like this two years ago?

One day, A Qing came in frantically, circling around my seat, barking shrilly.

"What's wrong, A Qing!"

He seemed to understand, suddenly turned around, and raised his back. I discovered that he had been injured. A large patch of hair was missing from his back, exposing raw, red flesh. Blood was dripping.

"A Qing! Why didn't you resist?" I asked. He raised his muzzle, wagged his tail pitifully, as if to say:

"I am old!"

The Tea Immortal 232

— Qian Zuizhu

Although he was used to drinking Wuyi tea that cost eight yuan a pound, in his current circumstances, even a packet of "family tea" costing ten copper coins plus two rosebuds already seemed quite flavorful.

"Enjoying wealth and enduring hardship, a true man can bend and stretch." These two old sayings were his comforting pill in his declining life. Therefore, even in a situation where suicide would be understandable, he could still live happily.

Coming back today, who knows what new hope he had gained? He held a freshly brewed cup of family tea in his hand, deeply pondering with relish. He stared at the cup as if it held some kind of Western spectacle, his eyes unblinking.

"Ha! Strange! One tea immortal is enough, let alone two." He was excitedly addressing the two tea stems standing upright in the cup. Then he muttered to himself, "One immortal is not surprising, but two tea stems standing together, isn't that something? Zhang Lao San promised to help me, Wang Lao Si promised to reply to me tomorrow. It looks like both things are promising."

He was so happy that he forgot himself and took a sip of tea. "Oh dear! Terrible! Both immortals have fallen!" He stomped his feet anxiously, scolding himself for being damned! Tomorrow, no matter what Lao San or Lao Si, not even a ghost will come to the door.

Wang Si Restaurant 233

— Yu Youqing

In my hometown, at the northern foot of Yushan Mountain, there is a Wang Si Restaurant, its fame is known to everyone, from the local gentry to the common laborers. Especially Wang Si's oil chicken, which is as famous as Beijing's Bianyifang roast duck. So, in the bright spring sunshine, Wang Si Restaurant opens for business in season, perhaps in line with the ancient poet's idea of buying wine in Xinghua Village.

I saw a poem by a certain gentleman in the local newspaper, the first two lines of which I have forgotten, but the third and fourth lines I still remember as "Wang Si Restaurant's flavor is good, yellow chicken white wine tender spinach green." His praise for Wang Si Restaurant is very appropriate. Indeed, in the third month of late spring, when the grass grows long in Jiangnan, tasting mountain delicacies and wild vegetables, drinking newly brewed village wine, is so flavorful. Life has few springs, so why not go and have fun, taste the village flavor!

I, a busy laborer, have long been at work when I encounter a spring holiday, thinking of the "yellow chicken white wine tender spinach green," I am still reluctant. I love Yushan, I love Wang Si Restaurant even more. People who love spring outings, when you come to Yushan, don't forget Wang Si Restaurant!

Shen Bao National Goods Special Edition

Issue Sixty-Seven (Published Every Thursday)

Contributions

Northwest National Goods Traveling Exhibition 234

— Yang Mang

Everyone knows that the Northwest is a region rich in resources, but few know that it is a place where foreign goods sell well. Therefore, anyone who has been to the Northwest says that the poor Northwest people, for the most part, do not know that many daily necessities are produced domestically. It is said that in the Northwest, they still use copper washbasins and wooden washbasins, still smoke British and American cigarettes, use Lion Brand Diamond Toothpaste, still wear American cloth, and wash with Xiangmao soap. In short, it is either completely local products or entirely foreign goods. If you tell them about domestic products, they simply do not believe it, thinking that Chinese goods could never be so advanced. Mr. Guo Weiping has traveled between the Northwest and Shanghai several times, and seeing this situation, he strongly urged the Shanghai national goods manufacturers to hold national goods exhibitions in various parts of the Northwest. Everyone agreed, and recently Mr. Guo, together with Mr. Zhao Bingren, a representative of the Shanghai factories, went to Kaifeng, Zhengzhou, Luoyang, Xi'an, Lanzhou and other places to negotiate, with very satisfactory results. Recently, Shanghai manufacturers will go to the Northwest together to hold mobile national goods exhibitions, bringing many good products here to the Northwest people, in order to arouse their purchasing psychology and confidence in liking domestic goods. Especially during Mr. Song Ziwen's engagement in the development of the Northwest, many conveniences can be obtained. Going to the Northwest has always been just a slogan, but now it is actually being realized by the national goods industry, which is enough to show the courage of the national goods industry. What the reporter hopes for is:

First, when going to the Northwest, do not just hold exhibitions and think that this is all you can do. You must go deep among the people and conduct practical investigations into their preferences and customs, what should be sold, and what does not meet their needs. Spend more time on interviews and observations. Roughly, in addition to the time used for the exhibition, half the time should be spent on the investigation part.

Second, contact local wholesalers as much as possible, give them various conveniences, reduce their doubts, and gain their sympathy, otherwise, you will create a bad impression and create resistance.

Third, when exhibiting in the interior, it is best to have multifaceted activities, such as banks, schools, government offices, and social organizations. Contact and talk to them, so that they have a thorough understanding, and then they can provide substantial help.

Going to the Northwest is a very interesting thing, and it is also a very labor-intensive and troublesome thing.

National Goods Talk

How Should Housewives Persuade Their Husbands to Use Domestic Goods? 235

— Ba Ling

This year is the publically designated National Goods Year for Women by various groups. All women in the country, regardless of age, whether wives, grandmothers, young ladies, female students, etc., should stand up to use and promote domestic goods, so that the domestic goods movement, through the advocacy, leadership, promotion, and use of women, can achieve a great effect. On the one hand, it can open up a new path for domestic goods, and at the same time, it can wash away the great shame of the general women, "Women are promoters of foreign goods."

Women themselves should vigorously use domestic goods in this year, but I think that many of the husbands of general women may still be obsessed with foreign goods and are unwilling to truly use domestic goods!

What should a woman who loves her country, loves her people, and loves her husband do when she encounters such a husband? What methods should she use to make her husband wholeheartedly use domestic goods and stop buying foreign goods? The following are some methods that I want to contribute. A housewife who loves to use domestic goods can follow these methods when she encounters a husband who does not love to use domestic goods. Although it cannot be said to be a panacea, it can at least achieve great results:

(1) When the husband buys things home, if they are foreign goods, he can refuse to use them.

(2) When the husband buys things home, you can say: "The thing is good, but unfortunately the money was seized by foreigners!"

(3) When the husband wants to buy something and consults with you, you can persuade him to buy domestic goods, and explain the advantages of using domestic goods.

(4) If the husband still buys foreign goods after you persuade him, you can refuse his requests.

Ladies, "A woman adorns herself for the one who pleases her." A wise housewife who is trusted by her husband, if her husband buys foreign goods, will surely be victorious if she does as the above methods suggest.

Women! Wake Up! 236

— Quan Jia

Women! When you haven't bought imported goods, you should think about it yourself.

If there are domestic goods for what you want to buy, why don't you buy domestic goods? Are you willing to be a slave to foreigners? Are you willing for your children and grandchildren to be slaves to foreigners? Maybe you think it doesn't matter to buy a few yuan, a few jiao, or even a few fen worth of foreign goods? You are completely wrong. You should read several famous sentences every day: "Foreign economic aggression amounts to more than 120 million yuan every year." Because you have domestic goods but don't buy them, the domestic goods industry will be completely bankrupt. Chinese goods factories are all built on the backs of Chinese people. If Chinese people don't buy them, who will buy them? You should guide your children to take the road of domestic goods. They are all masters of China!

If there are no domestic goods for what you buy, you should use them sparingly and especially should not waste them. When you see others wearing the most fashionable clothes, you should ask yourself in a low voice, "Those are all doing free advertising for foreigners!" If that thing is urgent, like medical supplies, etc., you should choose the cheaper one, but it is not goods for enemies.

Women! Don't sleep anymore. The outflow of domestic economy has shaken the national economy of domestic goods. We have the responsibility of guidance. In this Women's National Goods Year, let's do something!

National Goods Discussion

The Rise in Silver Prices and the Use of Domestic Goods 238

— Zhu Zhenmu

Ever since the news of the rise in silver prices spread from the gold standard countries, in recent days, many people with foresight and wisdom in our country's court and among the people have had many discussions, with differing opinions, but the degree of panic is actually the same. However, there are still many people in our country who are ignorant and not yet awakened from their spring sleep, and who does not have a greedy heart? Because silver prices have indeed risen, foreign exchange must be cheaper. Generally, fashionable ladies, wives, and compradors who sell imported goods will definitely take advantage of this cheap opportunity to engage in large-scale activities. Because the value of foreign goods that used to be one yuan can now be reduced to 70% or 80% below, that is, what used to be four pieces for one yuan can now be purchased for five pieces. Cheaper, cheaper, indeed a lot cheaper. However, the reporter has something to say. If we buy foreign goods, seeking temporary cheapness, and send out our limited silver desperately, to exchange for other people's surplus products, then in the future, the silver will be completely drained and fall into the hands of foreigners. Thus, the rural economy will not be able to circulate, the bank's funds will not be able to flow, the inner treasury will be empty, credit will go bankrupt, the market will be desolate, and all industries will collapse, even to the point where paper money is discounted, and agricultural products fall in price. A one-yuan banknote is actually worth eight jiao, and two yuan of grain may only be worth one and a half yuan. Invisibly, one-third of our assets will be lost. This is one example, but in reality it may be more than this, even below half is unpredictable. If so, the hidden losses can be predicted, and how can it be repaid by the small cheapness we seek today! Now, in order for the United States to promote its surplus inventory and expand its market in our country, it is bound to raise silver prices in order to increase our purchasing power. For the sake of their own interests, how can they stop? And the approval of the Silver Agreement will not have much effect on this. As for our government's restriction on the export of silver, although it is a good law, they can seal all the silver in foreign banks in our country, and transfer it separately. This is equivalent to the property of their country, without the name of shipping silver for export, but with the reality of outflow. It is still ineffective. Don't you see that the amount of silver currently stored in foreign banks in Shanghai has reached more than 270 million yuan, while the total amount of silver in Shanghai is only more than 56 million yuan, that is, only 120-130 million yuan in the whole country. That is, to this day, silver that has entered the hands of foreign merchants has already accounted for half of the total in Shanghai, and is about to reach one-quarter of the total in the country. Afterwards, if the silver price rises again and foreign exchange becomes cheaper, and the people of the country are greedy for small profits and buy foreign goods, letting their silver flow out, I am afraid that the disaster will not be far away. If we do not wake up, how can we save ourselves! Readers, if you are here, then even if the United States passes the increase in silver prices, the government approves the Silver Agreement, and the customs do not prohibit the export of silver, as long as all the people of the country do not buy foreign goods, follow the New Life Movement, and use domestic goods together, then they can only call in vain, and they can do nothing to us. I want my compatriots to pay attention, save the country and save the nation, is it not here!

Promoting Domestic Goods - Building Hankou as a Domestic Free City (Continued) 239

— Zhang Yanxiang

Our country's tariffs have long been declared autonomous by the government, but Hankou, the heart of the country's interior, has still not been able to obtain the benefits of autonomous tariffs, and is still suffering from it, leading to its decline. Goods transported by railway are not subject to tariffs, but goods transported by the Yangtze River, domestic goods entering and leaving must be taxed, and foreign goods entering and leaving are not taxed. Water transportation is cheaper than land transportation, so Hankou's domestic goods market cannot compete with foreign goods, because domestic goods must pay high transportation costs or double tariffs. According to the tariff system, Hankou's future will not benefit from the opening of the Yuehan Railway, but will only be a joint transportation point for the Pinghan and Yuehan railways, and only a small number of goods will be exchanged through this joint transportation point.

Therefore, for the sake of our country's domestic goods, for the sake of the Hankou market, and for the sake of the national industry and commerce, Hankou should be built as a domestic free city (the Hankou mentioned here refers to the broad sense of the area under the jurisdiction of the Jianghan Customs). All domestic goods transported from Hankou to any domestic port, Hankou and the arrival port, are exempt from tariffs, and all domestic goods transported from any domestic port to Hankou, the port of origin and Hankou are also exempt from tariffs, and foreign goods that have not been taxed by any of our country's customs, arriving in Hankou, or originating from Hankou, must still be taxed according to regulations. The domestic free city that I call is a free city that is inward-looking. Originally, it is not free to transport domestic goods domestically, so there is absolutely no need to talk about promoting domestic goods. I know the state of our country's central finances, I know the history of the customs system, I know that tax revenue is the foundation of public debt, I know the constraints of diplomatic treaties, but observing the future of our country's domestic goods, the position of industry and commerce in central China, and the recovery of the Hankou market, I believe that Hankou must be built as a domestic free city, so that it can be on par with the free city of Hong Kong, and Chicago as the second largest city. As for the actual steps and methods to solve various difficulties, it is up to the discussion of all sectors. (End)

National Goods News

A Visit to the Oriental New Red Electric Light Company Factory 240

— Fu Li

New Red lights have indeed become extremely popular in Shanghai in recent years. Whether it is in cinemas, dance halls, or various shops, they have already left their mark, because they are rich in beautiful and attractive colors. In the current metropolitan decorations of the twentieth century, they have indeed occupied a considerable position. Yesterday, the reporter was introduced by my old friend Mr. Xie and had the opportunity to visit the Oriental New Red Electric Light Company factory, which is run by Chinese people. After returning, I hastily recorded what I saw and heard.

According to Mr. Xie, the factory was established in the summer of the nineteenth year of the Republic. It was first established on Shishan Road in Zhabei. Later, due to the January 28th War, the entire factory was burned down, resulting in heavy losses. The manager is Mr. Zhang Huikang, who was originally an enthusiastic promoter of domestic goods. He is now also a director of the China National Goods Company and the manager of the Yaguang Electric Wood Company. Therefore, after the Oriental factory was destroyed, he set up a factory on Jing'an Temple Road and continued to operate. Now, a testing department has also been set up in the factory, and Mr. Huang Wenzhi, an engineer, has been hired to preside over everything in the factory. Mr. Huang graduated from Jiaotong University and has rich knowledge and experience. I heard that recently a kind of glass instrument has been successfully tested by Mr. Huang.

Page 18

In the near future, the factory will be able to produce its own products and recover the rights and interests. It is also good news in the National Goods Year.

The raw materials used by the factory to manufacture New Red lights, except for New Red gas and rubber wires, are all domestic products, such as glass tubes, transformers, etc. The factory is divided into six departments: tube bending, air extraction, lamp holder making, pattern making, painting, and wiring. There are about 50 workers, and tube bending and air extraction are the most difficult. Therefore, the workers in these two departments are all experienced technicians. Tube benders heat glass tubes about five feet long in a flame to soften them, and then slowly bend them according to the pattern, and blow them with their mouths to make them fat. There are three types of glass tubes: yellow, light yellow, and white. Yellow is used for making green and yellow lights. Light yellow is used for making light green lights. White is used for making blue and red lights. The thickness of the tube is also divided into several types, which are determined by the size of the character. This department's work is especially difficult in summer, because they work next to the fire and cannot open windows for ventilation. The wind will hinder the workers. It is very hard in the hot summer. I heard that the factory has a rule that if the temperature reaches above 94 degrees on the thermometer, they can stop working for one hour at noon, which is also to take care of the workers. Air extraction is more comfortable than tube bending. Just connect the bent character tube to the air extraction machine, extract the air in the tube to make it vacuum, heat the character tube with a powerful transformer, and then add a fixed amount, and light it for several hours on another transformer to make a dazzling New Red light of various colors.

For lamp holder making, pattern making, painting, wiring, etc., dozens of workers wear uniforms supplied by the company, neatly and uniformly, and work diligently. I deeply admire the factory's effective management and the harmony between labor and capital. The future is unlimited. Therefore, I wrote this visit record.

Necessary Countermeasures (Part 1) 243

— Lu Di

Today, the great disaster of our country, everyone knows it is the impoverishment of the people and the exhaustion of wealth. But where exactly lies the reason for causing this impoverishment of the people and exhaustion of wealth? In a word, it is due to the result of commercial and economic aggression by the great powers. In the past, many people were apprehensive about the great powers' military aggression being enough to destroy the country, because in their minds there was still the tragedy of severed heads and split intestines; but now, they are accustomed to and at ease with the commercial and economic aggression being enough to destroy the country, and they are calmly indifferent. Alas, who knows that this bone-scraping and marrow-sucking chronic pain is even worse than the tragedy of severed heads and split intestines in an instant?

The greatest enemy of our country's national products industry is none other than Japan. And recently, Japan's large-scale dumping of old rice, cotton cloth, matches, toys, and even sports equipment has gained momentum. If we do not devise countermeasures, the disaster of national subjugation is imminent. The purpose of this article is to first explore the reasons for Japan's recent dumping, and then seek countermeasures.

Japan's dumping of goods in our country is nothing new. It has existed since the beginning of the 20th century when that country's industry developed and transformed from an oppressed nation into an imperialist one. However, Japan's recent dumping has its own special reasons, which are described as follows.

(1) Compensation for Export Trade: Japan's exports to China have always been smooth. In 1925, they accounted for about one-third of our country's total trade, and in 1930, they also accounted for one-third. In other words, it has long occupied the top spot. However, since that year, it has shown a decline. After the Eastern Provinces Incident and the Shanghai War, our country strongly resisted Japanese goods, and Japan's trade with China gradually declined. By last year, it had fallen to fourth place, behind England, America, and Australia. For Japan, a country based on industry and commerce, the decline in trade is undoubtedly a fatal injury. It is appropriate that they are now desperately dumping to seek a comeback.

(2) Crisis of Financial Deficit: Finance is an indicator of a country's economic prosperity. Looking at Japan's budget for this year, expenditures reached 2.9 billion yuan, with a deficit of several hundred million yuan. Public debt is the best means to alleviate the deficit. However, Japan's public debt was 700 million yuan last year and increased to 900 million yuan this year. In fact, whether society can bear it is questionable. Is it not the dream of the entire country of Japan to strive to develop foreign trade and shift its economic panic to other countries?

(3) Opposition to Economic Bloc: The division of current economic blocs has become the most obvious thing. Japan's foreign trade, in addition to our country, is strongest with South America and India. Today, India's trade is very unfavorable to Japan, and South America has also been snatched away by Roosevelt's hand. Even Japan, which is as stubborn as it is, cannot help but sigh in vain. Now there is a country that is very close in distance, has a great need for cheap goods, and has no weapons to resist the import of foreign goods. Moreover, this hunting ground has not yet been included in the "bloc" range of other great powers. Is this not the peach blossom spring of Japanese goods?

After the Great Comparison Period, the Foreign Market is Light Beyond Constant 247

In the past few days, it was the end of the fourth big comparison period, with a large amount of inflow and outflow, and the situation was prosperous, but the actual situation was very tragic. Various industries could not get the real benefits of adjustment and abundance, and the tax rates felt exhausted and unbearable, resulting in a sluggish market atmosphere in various industries, and there was no possibility of activity. Free Talk

Research on "Fangjinqi" (Scholar-Official Air) (3) 267

— Lin Yutang

Because Western modern culture has a natural and lively view of life, and has undergone the liberation of the 19th-century Romantic movement, Western modern culture is more tolerant and more humane. I believe this is a sign of the healthy spirit of Western nations. Although new culture has been promoted in China, it has not been refined by decades of Romanticism, so people's hearts are still depressed, and people's minds are still dry. As soon as there is danger, everyone bursts into a flurry of firecrackers, which disappears like a flash in the pan after five minutes, because people's hearts are fundamentally unhealthy, and the balance between joy and sorrow is lost. Crying out in pain may seem more sincere and patriotic than smiling or being occasionally comfortable, but unfortunately, after crying out until one's throat is dry, the breath cannot be sustained, and silence follows crying, like a child falling asleep after crying. Although occasionally groaning once or twice in the silence, it is the moaning of a sick poplar, a sour, corrupt, and decadent sound. In today's literature, it seems that there are no loud shouts, only sneaking in the dark to release a few cold arrows. But people's psychology is always self-righteous, so there is a habit of sucking... One feels weak oneself, and hates that others are healthy. One's own actions are evil, and one is jealous of others' liveliness. One drinks water oneself, and one is jealous of others drinking tea. One groans oneself, and one hates others' laughter. It is always due to a lack of generosity in the heart. For two thousand years, the "fangjinqi" spirit has still pressed down on the 20th-century vernacular writers, making it impossible for them to breathe. As a result, only a buzzing sound can be heard in literature.

The so-called natural and lively Western view of life can be illustrated with new examples. For example, playing is natural. In the past, Confucian academies forbade children from playing. Now, educational concepts have been liberated and are closer to nature. As a result, not only is playing not forbidden, but kindergartens, primary schools, and middle schools use play to nurture children's virtues. Western couples are affectionate and travel hand-in-hand, simply acknowledging that the pleasures of men and women are something that humans should have and do not need to disguise. Therefore, they generously walk hand-in-hand on the street without feeling strange. From the Chinese perspective, one can only secretly envy the "foreign devils" for knowing how to enjoy sensual pleasures. But once Chinese people also become liberated in terms of male-female relations, it is considered unacceptable, and said to be harmful to social customs. Seeing Western men and women bathing naked in the sea and playing in the water, one may also envy them, but seeing Chinese men and women bathing naked in the sea, one must immediately scold them for corrupting social morals. Western women's clothing may be very seductive, but no one in modern Western criticism has said that they are harmful to public morals, because they already have some tolerance from the Romantic movement. However, when Chinese people see Western women in seductive and glamorous clothing, they may admire them, but when they see Chinese women in the same kind of clothing, they will scold them for being "modern." Western stage dances, such as the grass skirt dance, are a hundred times more perverse than anything in China, but it has never been heard that Western thinkers have criticized them. In fact, Westerners have not forgotten to love their country as a result of watching the grass skirt dance. Chinese people cannot tolerate the grass skirt dance, putting on a moralistic face and scolding it as a sign that people's hearts are greatly changed and the world is in great chaos. However, Chinese people have not become morally superior or their country richer and stronger as a result of their strict lives. The whole country is filled with a kind of gloomy, moldy, hypocritical, and pedantic atmosphere. Therefore, these "fangjinqi" critics, even while groaning under oppression themselves, scolding "cultural unification," and complaining about "news censorship," will oppress others as soon as they become news censors themselves. I saw my daughter watching two bedbugs arguing on the bed board. One scolded the other, "You are a bedbug!" And the other scolded back, "You are a bedbug!" I hid to the side and laughed heartily.

Because their hearts are fundamentally unhealthy and their lives lack the courage to move forward, "fangjinqi" critics are only good at destruction. When faced with advocating the natural and lively Western view of life, they can only denigrate and cannot build. They criticize the Analects, saying "China has no humor." If China had humor long ago, why would there be a need to promote it by publishing the Analects? Shouting "China has no humor" from the sidelines will not cause the roots of humor to gradually flourish. Moreover, even if the Analects does not have successful works of humor, it has at least changed the attitude of the Chinese people towards humor. Unless one is a novice who is still paying attention to the "Great Way" of the universe and saving the country, everyone has a deeper understanding of humor. Only a few people who have a superficial and incomplete understanding cannot accept the Western culture's attitude towards humor. This kind of passive and destructive criticism, while claiming to promote Western culture, actually hinders Western culture, and will not itself achieve solid results. When *Ren Jian Shi* ("This Human World") was published, it stirred up the "hang yu hang yu" faction's "fangjinqi." They flailed their arms and legs, blowing wildly, but did not move *Ren Jian Shi* in the slightest. There was not even a decent critique of the content and editing of *Ren Jian Shi* that I could humbly accept. For example, I myself thought that there were too many articles about flowers, trees, spring light, and travel in the first issue, which was unsatisfactory, but no one pointed this out. In short, there was not a single piece of writing that I thought was worthy of criticizing *Ren Jian Shi*. Only the attack on Zhou Zuoren's poetry was a critique of content, but it was laughably shallow, only attacking a private individual. What is the error of *Ren Jian Shi*? I know... Using Song typeface is too archaic. In the eyes of a "fangjinqi" critic, this is an unforgivable crime.

Editor's note: If the debate about humor, etc., continues to develop, it is feared that it will be far from "humor." It is proposed to end this here for the best.

For Self and For Others 268

— Shi Fa

When a novelist writes a novel and an artist creates art, their starting point is centered on themselves, embracing an attitude of "I am the only one worthy of respect in heaven and on earth." They truly feel that even if the heavens collapse and the earth cracks, it will not move my hammer or paintbrush. Moreover, the world will come to an end after I have fully expressed my abilities. Only then can there be great creation.

However, when working for society, promoting an idea, or guiding young people, the approach is completely different. This is almost entirely for others! Although one cannot be without oneself when working for others, one must always think of others, society, and humanity. It is also worthwhile to consider the current situation, take into account the future, and consider the methods of expression.

It seems that many great figures today have not noticed this point. Perhaps in the midst of chaos, they have not realized their own influence and power. After a word is spoken, the effect is minimal, like a wheel axle, while the resulting movement is large, like the wheel. As a certain gentleman once said, turning in the center and following the perimeter, one is forever busy, wasting effort and achieving nothing. That analogy is indeed accurate.

Much of the energy of some young people has been wasted in vain, following the adults and teachers in shouting slogans and running around. As a result, the leaders often end up in a situation where the present self is fighting with yesterday's self, at most lightly admitting mistakes, while the common people suffer, bleeding and dying. The mistake is that they used to purely express themselves based on emotion. Now they are trying hard to make up for it, but how can they make up for it? And today's self may fight with tomorrow's self again, so the situation is even more dangerous!

The rapid reversals and repetitions of Japan's Westernization and its subsequent return to tradition, and the revolution followed by the worship of Buddha, have resulted in countless sacrifices. It is not until many leaders gradually reach old age, their knowledge richer than it is now, and their temperament more peaceful, that they recall what they did in the past and secretly exclaim, "Shame! Shame!"

There may be many emerging leaders. Whatever they are advocating, it is worthwhile to consider the current state of this era and the future impact. The beginning is simple, but the end is great. There is ruthless history and unforeseen facts behind it, which must be carefully considered!

Essays and Novels 269

— Mu Mutian

Essays and novels are two different literary genres (Genre Litteraire). Of course, there exist neutral things between the two. However, the distinction between the two is clearly visible.

These two different literary genres are mutually related. "The river water does not interfere with well water" is very rare in the world. However, their social basis at the time of origin (Origin) is different. And, that refers to the origin of the genre. It is not to say that, thereafter, those who write prose essays are certainly entirely from the scholar-official class, while those who write novels are certainly entirely from the citizen class. However, in prose essays, reflecting the leisurely thoughts of the idle, is the majority. Why can so many prose essays be produced among British writers who are gentlemen (Gentlemen)? The realists from the citizen class, like Zola, Flaubert, and others, don't write many prose essays, do they? This is something we cannot but study from the relationship between genre and social life.

I believe that these two different genres should independently seek their own development prospects. If, as Mr. Xu Weiyong said, "writers with fulfilling lives" "use the strength to wrestle lions to write prose essays," needless to say, prose essays will have a great future. However, are such writers only a very small minority? Are there some prose essay writers who, because other paths are blocked, go to prose essays to find an escape route? The tendency of "novelization of essays" contains elements of retreat. The pursuit of a fulfilling life is the fundamental method to resolve this tendency of retreat, needless to say. However,

On Writing (II) 270

— Cao Juren

Mr. Zhang Taiyan said: "All argumentation should be based on reputable authorities, not on sophistry. To rely on arrogance when words are inadequate, to wander in rage and pique, trampling on crops and vegetables, ultimately leading to self-contradiction in several chapters, is something the ancients did not do." "A type of work, divided, becomes several chapters; combined, it is only one chapter, with an inherent and well-ordered system. Sima Qian's Records of the Grand Historian is divided into five categories: Annals, Hereditary Houses, Biographies, Treatises, and Tables. The Annals and Tables serve as the warp, and the Hereditary Houses and Biographies serve as the weft. Warp and weft complement each other, forming a seamless great work. Zhuangzi's "Wandering Freely," "Discussion on Equalizing All Things," and "Nourishing the Lord of Life" three chapters, when viewed together, are also just one great work. Great works are difficult to organize. Throughout history, those worthy of being called "works" are, apart from the philosophers of the pre-Qin period, only Wang Chong's Discourses Weighed in the Balance, Liu Xie's The Literary Mind and the Carving of Dragons, Liu Zhiji's General Principles of Historiography, and Zhang Xuecheng's General Principles of Literature and History, just so few. The modern world of writing appears exceptionally barren, which also shows the general weakness of organizational ability!"

Gu Tinglin himself said that in his life of reading, whatever he gained, he would record it; if there were disagreements, he would revise it from time to time; if the ancients had it before him, then he would delete it. "If the ancients had it before me, then I would delete it." This means that without unique insights, one cannot form one's own school of thought, and there is no need for writing. In recent times, there have been several dozen types of histories of Chinese literature, varied and diverse, published. If we want to meticulously write a history of literature, we should see how others have organized their histories of literature. If our own opinions are completely the same as theirs, then we should not write. If most are the same, but a small part is different, it is enough to write "Notes on Differences in a Certain History of Literature." Mr. Lu Xun, in his lecture in Guangzhou, "The Demeanor of the Wei and Jin Dynasties and the Relationship between Articles, Medicine, and Wine," at the beginning, cited Liu Shipei's History of Medieval Literature, saying, "If Mr. Liu's book is already detailed, I will be brief"; conversely, "what Mr. Liu is brief on, I will be more detailed." This method of being detailed where the other is brief and mutually elucidating can be said to be the most enlightened approach. If this method is followed, most of those monotonous histories of literature on the market can be discarded.

In the past, people often wrote annotations for ancient books, and annotations are also works. Liu Xiaobiao annotated A New Account of Tales of the World, complementing the original text by Liu Yiqing. Pei Songzhi annotated Chen Shou's Records of the Three Kingdoms, "What Shou did not record, matters that should be preserved, he would take in full to fill the gaps. Or, if the same event was described in different terms, or if the events originated from different sources and doubts could not be resolved, he would copy and include them to provide different accounts." With the talent of Liu Xiaobiao and Pei Songzhi, could they not have written their own books? Yet they only made themselves known through annotations. Writing is for the public good, there is no need to set up a separate banner to elevate oneself. For example, Zheng Kangcheng's compilation and annotation of the Classics broke the divide between the Old and New Text schools. Zhu Xi's annotation of the Four Books expounded many genuine insights of Neo-Confucianism. Annotations have the same value as original works.

Three.

Recently, I read Fang Dongshu's Shulin Yang Kui, (a person from Tongcheng, Qing Dynasty), which still quotes previous people's comments on writing and literature, saying, "Writing books and establishing theories must be born out of necessity, only then will the words be appropriate, credible, and useful; therefore, the words of a gentleman reach the principles of things and stop there, not engaging in elaborate rambling, unrestrained grandstanding, taking pleasure in the moment." Another said: "What cannot be cut off from the world is the way of enlightenment, the recording of political affairs, the consoling of the people's troubles, and the delighting in the goodness of others. If such things are beneficial to the world and beneficial to the future, then one article, one more article of benefit." It can be said that the ancients regarded solving social problems and life problems as the sole purpose of writing, as the saying goes, "I would rather record it in practical actions than in empty words." This attitude of writing for life is quite worthy of our approval. However, this attitude is most difficult to maintain: the various schools of thought in the Warring States period each displayed their own ideas, speaking practical words. Qin Shihuang unified the world with Legalism, leaving only the sayings of alchemists and immortals. The pre-Qin Confucians valued integrity most, not straying far from benevolence and righteousness. However, the Western Han Confucians abandoned Confucius and Mencius's ideas of helping the world, painting over them with the colors of yin-yang theory to please the emperor. In the early Qing Dynasty, the great Confucians Gu, Huang, Yan, and Wang, used their knowledge of the classics for practical application, waiting in darkness for a wise ruler to visit, saying, "For the demise of the world, every commoner is responsible." Once the literary inquisitions of Qianlong and Jiaqing arose one after another, scholars only spoke of textual interpretations and dared not discuss worldly affairs at all. Since the First Sino-Japanese War, the ideological world has experienced strong stimulation, and social and life problems have become the center of discussion several times. This type of writing has also been popular like waves, sometimes selling a lot (during the years of Guangxu 27-28 and the Republic of China 9-10 and 17-18, this type of writing was printed everywhere). Now it has turned into a popular period for the Siku Quanshu and the Gujin Tushu Jicheng, "Writing for life" is a path that is not passable, whether in ancient or modern times!

Defense is also quite necessary. However, only making a defense of style without pursuing a fulfilling life will naturally lead to being lost in the fog.

I believe that since the May Fourth Movement, the acquisition of citizen rights by the "novel" is the greatest success in the literary movement. "Novel" is the most important literary style of the past ten years. The groundbreaking contribution of "Call to Arms" will probably forever shine brightly in the history of Chinese literature. If one says that "the only success of modern Chinese literature in the past fourteen years is the success of the essay," then it is a bit of an exaggeration. And the statement that "creative novels, even good ones, come from the training of small essays," if only from the point of view of the cultivation of style (Style), it is not impossible, but this statement can easily mislead some people into thinking that writing good essays makes the creation of novels easy. I think that from the origin of the genre, "novel" is not derived from the small essay. (To be continued)

Letter to the Editor 271

Brother Liewen:

After reading Mr. Lin Yutang's letter in today's "Free Talk," I cannot remain silent, so I am sending a few words. Lin Yutang's target is entirely me. Now that the curtain has been lifted, I believe there is nothing to avoid, and I must defend myself. I had heard rumors in Shanghai that Lin Yutang was planning a general attack on me, but I had never offended him, so I dared not believe it. Now it has become a reality, leaving me at a loss as to the cause. I have been watching lanterns in Xiashi for four or five days, and continuous rain has delayed my trip. Yesterday it finally cleared up, and my spirits were slightly better. Unexpectedly, I have been dragged into a whirlpool of right and wrong hundreds of miles away. Lin Yutang said that I systematically attacked "Ren Jian Shi" in "Ren Yan," "Ten Days' Talk," "Maodun Monthly," "China Daily," and "Free Talk" under pseudonyms. What evidence does he have? I wrote an article on essays and sketches in "Maodun Monthly," but what is the reason that the other articles must be written by me? If Lin Yutang does not have strong and truthful evidence to prove that the other articles were indeed written by me, he cannot escape the malicious intent of fabricating, creating, and framing me. Why Lin Yutang has such a vicious heart is something I cannot understand now. After watching the lanterns, I will return to Shanghai to investigate the cause and clarify the truth to the world in order to clear my name. If Lin Yutang can reflect on himself, discover his humanity, and be moved by his conscience, he will surely reverse his malicious and harmful thoughts. Then he should have the courage to correct his mistakes, repent sincerely, and apologize to the public. Please publish this letter as it is, because I also want to show Lin Yutang a way to renew himself. Written hastily, no second copy. Zhang Kebiao, April 30th, in Xiashi.

A Novel of the Middle Ages (V) 272

— Written by Mark Twain of America (Translated by Zun Han)

Gong Na helplessly stretched out his scepter, while in his robe, his woman's heart felt very compassionate for the fate of this unfortunate criminal. Tears welled up in his eyes. He opened his mouth to speak, but the Minister of Justice hurriedly said to him, "Don't say it there, Your Highness, don't say it there! It is illegal to pronounce a sentence on a scion of the Duke without sitting on the Duke's throne."

Poor Gong Na shivered. Old Kruggenstein's steel bones also trembled. Gong Na had not yet been crowned! Did he dare to defile the throne? He hesitated and turned around, his face pale with fear. But he had to go. Some people had already cast surprised glances at him. If he hesitated any longer, those glances would become suspicious. He ascended the steps of the throne. Then he stretched out his scepter and said:

"Defendant, I now perform my duties in the name of our lord, Duke Wuli of Brandenburg. Listen to me. According to the ancient laws of the country, you can only be spared death if you hand over your accomplice to the executioner. You can take advantage of this opportunity for rescue. Save yourself, if that is possible; tell the name of the father of that child!"

A grave silence fell upon this highest court, a silence so deep that even the beating of people's hearts could be heard. The Princess slowly turned around, her eyes shining with resentment, and pointed at Gong Na with the index finger of her right hand, saying:

"The father of this child is you."

The painful belief of encountering an irredeemable and hopeless disaster made Gong Na's heart shudder as if dead. What power in the world could save him? To defend himself, he would have to declare that he was originally a woman, but a woman who had not been crowned and defiled the throne would also be sentenced to death. Therefore, he and his violent old father fainted together on the ground.

XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX

Whether here or elsewhere, we cannot find the next installment of this heart-stirring and tragic story, not today, and not ever.

The truth is because I put my protagonist (or heroine) in a particularly impossible situation, so I can't think of any way to make him (or her) tell. And I don't want to deal with this matter now either. He should tell himself,

－－－－or leave him there. I originally thought this small difficulty was resolvable, but I changed my mind. (The End)
