Husband-Seeking Corps 273

— Chen

During this time of bright spring and pleasant scenery, many women are falling into spring sorrow and boudoir complaints. The so-called "Suddenly seeing the color of the willows on the roadside, regretting having taught my husband to seek a title" is precisely the case. This is just the sadness of heroes, beauties, talented scholars, and beautiful women. Their self-seeking troubles stem from their own deep dreams of being ennobled, or are caused by being moved by the scenery. Those who do not originate from romantic feelings and intentions, but actually "grieve for spring," cannot be compared to these ladies. The Austrian Husband-Seeking Corps is a recent example.

According to a Lin Zi telegram from the Guomin News Agency on the 13th: "Today, hundreds of Japanese women, each carrying their children, flocked to the Prosecutor's Office, begging for the release of their husbands, because their husbands were arrested and imprisoned during the February Incident... The Upper Austrian Governor then met with them, and fifty people represented them. In addition to stating their suffering, the representatives also said that they had no money to buy food and asked for relief." This husband-seeking action is naturally incomparable to those who have a feeling of being咫尺天涯, because they have the enormous threat of having no money to buy food in addition to "suffering."

From this incident, we are reminded of the "decisive action" of the geta-wearing friends in Manchuria a couple of years ago, when the policy of non-resistance was also on the rise. The geta-wearing women of Tokyo, because their husbands had long been conscripted and could not bear the taste of "empty beds and lonely nights," also had a husband-seeking action. Although the traces are close to the feelings of children, the husbands are being restrained by others, losing their freedom, and unable to fly together, leading to the act of sitting and seeking at the door.

If we were to follow the social morality of a Chinese village school, breaking up a couple would damage one's yin virtue, and helping someone to achieve happiness would be better than building a pagoda. Then these politicians have created a large number of resentful men and women who will never be able to escape their blame. However, from the perspective of the new social outlook, we should not criticize this action based solely on its morality. We should examine the universality of this phenomenon, what objective causes have formed it, and how to eliminate these problems.

Clearly, the current social system in various countries, which is cloaked in democracy, is essentially ruled by a minority. All the facilities of national administration are only used to uphold their interests. They use the form of political power to turn their own private wishes into "public interests," and forcefully praise their own attempts as the will of the people. Under this method, countless tragedies of separated families have been enacted in the current society, but they are considered legitimate and justified. For example, under the pressure of hunger and cold, the lives of most people are already uneasy, and society is already uneasy. However, in the name of maintaining peace, they infringe on the freedom of the people as much as possible, and deprive the people of the opportunity to survive as much as possible. As a result, countless orphans and widows are produced. The so-called "peace" is only their own "peace" of infinite enjoyment. Again, like the many wars between nations, it is clearly many financial giants who are forcibly seizing the market and openly robbing, but they want to put some high hats of national glory and victory of the motherland under the form of the nation, so that countless women who have lost their sons and husbands do not criticize because of "glory" and "victory." But this lofty ideal of "raping public opinion" cannot be understood or trusted by every woman. This is why Japanese and Austrian women are asking for bread and work, and there is a husband-seeking action.

At this moment, the sound of world unrest is frequently heard, and the international situation is also particularly urgent. It is unknown how many women's husbands will be forcibly taken away. If we do not break these thoughts of national glory and attitudes of lingering on, then many men will become cannon fodder, and there will be nowhere to seek them back. What is more, if we want to fundamentally eliminate the phenomenon of sacrificing the majority of men for the interests of a minority, that is, to eliminate the phenomenon of husband-seeking, then we can only destroy the system that takes one's own selfish desires as the will of the public.

"Pitiful are the bones by the ever-changing river, still the people in deep boudoirs dreaming." Thinking of this scene on the eve of the Great War already makes people shudder. In addition, many adults regard imprisonment as the only way to maintain peace. Take precautions, prepare in advance, and may countless women who will step into "husband-seeking" encourage each other.

The Naming Question 274

— Wang Ci

On the 24th, the typesetter of this journal joked with me and arranged the characters "主慈" (Zhu Ci) into "王慰" (Wang Wei) -- the name of an article "青青" (Qing Qing) -- in fact, this is a very ordinary thing: but, strangely enough,巧不巧 (qiao bu qiao), "王慰" (Wang Wei) is my sister's name. When my sister saw it, she wrote a letter and said:

"You little devil! Why are you using my name to publish your boring text?"

After reading the letter, I laughed heartily.

In fact, for us poor scholars, as long as we can see our own words published; as long as we can receive the royalties for each article every month, that is already enough! The matter of naming is really carefree. It is lucky enough to be able to keep the surname passed down by our ancestors without omitting it, which is already satisfactory. Even if the surname is Zhang or Pan, we would never covet it.

Regarding the issue of naming, I have three friends with different personalities:

The first friend's surname is Zhao. He can write articles of the "historical" type. His naming is entirely something like "生" (Sheng), "女史" (Nushi). He said:

"If I used my real name, I would definitely be called 'XX Doctor'!"

The second friend's surname is Xu. His production of sketches is extremely large, but he has countless aliases, writing an article as "XX" and another article as "○○". He said:

"My own things are written too sloppily, wouldn't it be terrible if I didn't do this!"

The third friend's surname is Hu. He writes very good novels about triangular love affairs. Once he finishes an article, he sells it to the famous writer Zhang XX for the price of two yuan per thousand words. When publishing a single volume, the name is of course Zhang XX. He said:

"Is a prostitute's selling of chastity her own sin?"

I've talked too much. In short, if the typesetter of this journal looks at this completely boring thing of mine and feels a little apologetic, then I want to answer:

"Brother! What are you talking about! What are you talking about! I don't mind! I don't mind!"

The Mystery of "Animated Divination Diagram" 275

— He Juefu

— One of the University Scenes —

In recent days, the dozen or so classmates who live with me in this small building have inexplicably started another commotion. Whether it is in the morning, in the evening, in the plaza, or in the dormitory, as long as three or five people gather together, they are talking about this with great interest:

"It's really strange. You say we are using our own fingers to exert force, so the small tile can move. Why can it also point to characters very clearly? And, our fingers are only lightly touching it, and no force is being used at all."

"Of course! It's not our fingers exerting force; however, this is a bit mysterious, and our intelligence cannot understand it."

"Think about it, China did not lack great diviners in the past; however, it was only because no one passed it down that we have ended up in a situation where everyone is confused. For example, this simplest 'Animated Divination Diagram' was originally something that existed in ancient China. Even now that science has reached its extreme, haven't people still not understood it?"

"Yes, that kind of 'Animated Divination Diagram...'." I didn't understand what they were talking about at all, but I felt a little strange in my heart. Later, I asked Lao Lin in private, and he told me the details here:

The "Animated Divination Diagram" is a tool for divination of good and bad fortune. This diagram was created by a certain scholar who studied in Germany, who spent many years researching spiritualism, and improved the old methods inherent in our country. Its style is: a square white paper, three feet on each side, with a strange large human shape of about one and a half inches in diameter drawn in the middle. Around the human shape, there are more than two thousand characters surrounding it. To divine, a small tile with a diameter and a shape similar to that of the circle in the middle is placed upside down in the center of the circle. And an arrowhead shape is drawn on the edge of the tile to be used for pointing to characters. Then, three people use the middle fingers of their three right hands to lightly press on the bottom of the tile, while reciting this spell: "Please, Tile Brother, call XX (whether dead or alive) to come and talk." After half an hour has passed, the small tile will slowly move. (The fingers should naturally not be released.) At this time, you can ask whatever you want, and it can very clearly point to the characters to reply."

After Lao Lin told me these things, he said very seriously:

"It's really effective! If you don't believe it, you can try it. The day before yesterday, I told those Shandong guys in Room X, and at first they didn't believe it. It wasn't until yesterday that they bought it back and personally experimented with it that they believed what I said. Alas! This is really a bit mysterious. I heard that at XX University, almost every student is playing with this thing. The school authorities, in order to maintain the school's reputation, are about to issue a notice to ban it!"

What exactly is going on, I haven't personally experimented with it, so of course I don't dare to say; but, many university students are actually fascinated by this, and I don't quite understand it. Is it that what college students do now is originally something that other people don't understand?
